bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ Gusunɔ u hɑnduniɑ toruɑ, u wɔllu kɑ tem tɑkɑ
bba	wee tɛ̃, wini u wɑsi mɔ nɡe nɛɡii mɑm mɑm.
bba	Kɑɑ n dɑ mɑwɑ kɑ nɔni swɑ̃ɑru.
bba	Mɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u kpɑm nɛɛ, mbɑ ɑ kuɑ mi. Wunɛn wɔnɔn
bba	yɛm mɛ mu yɑri temɔ, mu nɛn lɑɑkɑri seeye.
bba	Enɔsin mɑrubun biru, Sɛti wi, u bii tɔn durɔbu kɑ tɔn
bba	kurɔbu mɑrumɔ sere n kɑ kuɑ wɔ̃ɔ nɛnɛ kɑ nɔɔbɑ
bba	Mɑ win ɡɔ̃ru ɡɑ sɑnkirɑ yèn sɔ̃ u tɔmbu tɑkɑ kuɑ
bba	hɑnduniɑɔ. Yɑ nùn duɑ too sere win nukurɔ.
bba	15-16 Hunde koni bɑɑyere kpuro ɡesi, yɑ duɑwɑ kɑ Nɔwɛ
bba	sɑnnu ɡoo ɡe sɔɔ yiru yiru dwɑɑ kɑ niɑ, nɡe mɛ
bba	Gusunɔ u Nɔwɛ sɔ̃ɔwɑ. Mɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u nùn kɛnusi.
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ Nɔwɛn tɑm mu kpɑllɑ, yerɑ u nuɑ ye win bii
bba	Yi dɑ dɑ Sidoniɔ, Gerɑn berɑ ɡiɑ sere kɑ Gɑsɑɔ kɑ
bba	mɑɑ Sodomuɔ kɑ Gomɔrɑ ɡiɑ kɑ Adimɑ kɑ Seboimuɔ n kɑ
bba	Heberu u kuɑ wɔ̃ɔ tɛnɑ kɑ nnɛ mɑ u Pelɛɡi mɑrɑ.
bba	Nɑ nun kɑnɑmɔ, ɑ nɛɛ, wunɛ nɛn sesuwɑ kpɑ bu ku mɑn
bba	wɑhɑlɑ ko wunɛn sɔ̃, kpɑ ɑ wɑ ɑ nɛn wiru dwe.
bba	Yerɑ wɔ̃ɔ wɔkurɑ nnɛse, Kedolɑmɛɛ kɑ sinɑm be bɑ

bba	Asiterɔtu Kɑɑnɑimuɔ, mɑ bɑ Susibɑ tɑbu di Hɑmuɔ, mɑ
bba	bɑ Emibɑ tɑbu di Sɑfe Kiriɑtɑimuɔ.
bba	Yerɑ Aburɑmu u yɛɛ yi kpuro mɛnnɑ u yi ɡo u bɛrɑnɑ
bba	yiru u yin bɛsi yi u kɑrinɑsiɑ, ɑdɑmɑ u ǹ ɡunɔsu
bba	Kon kɑ nun ɑrukɑwɑni bɔke kpɑ n wunɛn bweseru dɑbiɑsiɑ
bba	Kon dɑ n dĩɑnu tɑmɑ fiiko kpɑ i di i kɑ dɑm wɑ. Yen
bba	biru kpɑ i sere swɑɑ wɔri i doonɑ. Bɛɛn nɑɑ te, tɑ
bba	bɛɛrɛ kuɑ. Yen sɔ̃, i de i nɛn yɑɑrɛ di.
bba	Mɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u nɛɛ, kon wuu ɡe deri ɡen tɔnu weeru yen
bba	Wuu ɡeni wee, ɡɑ wɑ̃ɑ turuku, ɡɑ ǹ mɑɑ kpɑ̃. A de
bba	n dɑ n kuke mi, kpɑ n fɑɑbɑ wɑ. Ye u wɑ ɡɔrɑdo wi, u
bba	ǹ wisɑ, mɑ u nɛɛ, nɡe ɡɑ ǹ piibu sɑ̃ɑ ro?
bba	Mɑ Aburɑhɑmu u wisɑ u nɛɛ, nɑ rɑɑ tɑmɑɑ bɑ ǹ
bba	Gusunɔn bɛrum mɔwɑ tem mini, kpɑ bu mɑn ɡo nɛn kurɔn
bba	Adɑmɑ u Abimɛlɛki ɡerusi dɔkɔ ɡɑɑn sɔ̃ ye
bba	Abimɛlɛkin yobu bɑ nùn mwɑɑri.
bba	yèn sɔ̃ ɑ kuɑ mɛ, mɑ ɑ ǹ kɑ mɑn wunɛn bii teere te
bba	yinɑri, nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔ nɑ bɔ̃rumɔ kɑ nɛn tiin yĩsiru
bba	Sɔ̃ɔ teeru u win yobun tɔnwero wi u win yɛnun dukiɑ kpuro

bba	Ye u turɑ mi, u nɛɛ, ɑ seewo su dɑ yɛnuɔ, wunɛ wi Yinni
bba	Gusunɔ u domɑru kuɑ. Mbɑn sɔ̃nɑ kɑɑ n yɔ̃ tɔɔwɔ.
bba	Wɔɔ, nɑ nun ɑyeru kuɑ yɛnuɔ kɑ wunɛn yooyoosuɡiru

bba	woodɑbɑ swĩi ye nɑ nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ kpuro.
bba	Yen tɔ̃ɔ terɑ Isɑkin yobu bɑ nɑ bɑ nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ bɑ

bba	u ɡinɑ nɛɛ, wunɑ nɛn bii Esɑu kɑ ɡem?
bba	Adɑmɑ ɑ̀ n dɑ kɑ tii yinɑ,
bba	Mɑ Yɑkɔbu u seewɑ u win sɑnum wɔri u dɑ sɔ̃ɔ yɑri

bba	kɑnɛ. À n dɑɑ mɑn sɔ̃ɔwɑ, kon de ɑ doonɑ kɑ nuku

bba	kuɑ. Yen biru u ɡɔsirɑ u wurɑ win yɛnuɔ.
bba	Yerɑ durɔ wi, u bikiɑ u nɛɛ, ɑmɔnɑ wunɛn yĩsiru.

bba	29-30 Beniwɑ bɑ kuɑ Horibɑn bwese kɛrin wiruɡibu Edɔmun

bba	Efɑrɑtɑ yerɑ bɑ mɔ̀ Bɛtelehɛmu.

bba	Mɔwisi u nɛɛ, too, yɑ wɑ̃, ɑ ǹ mɑɑ mɑn wɑsi.
bba	Sɔ̃ɔ nɔɔbɑ yiru yen bɑɑ sɔɔ, bu ku rɑɑ pɛ̃ɛ
bba	seeyɑtiɑ wɑ bɛɛn yɛnusɔ. Domi wi u ɡɑ̃ɑnu di ni bɑ
bba	seeyɑtiɑ doke, bɑ koo yɛ̃ro ɡowɑ, bɑɑ ù n sɔɔn nɑ.
bba	Isirelibɑ kpurowɑ bɑ koo tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑ te di.

bba	Yinni Gusunɔ deriɑ. Gisɔ i ǹ ye wɑsi temɔ.
bba	Sɑɑ ye sɔɔ, Yetoro Mɑdiɑnibɑn yɑ̃ku kowo, wi u sɑ̃ɑ

bba	tɔmbu Isirelibɑ kuɑ sɑnɑm mɛ u bu yɑrɑmɑ Eɡibitin di.

bba	ko ko nɛn tiin tɔmbu n tɔmbu kpuro kere. Hɑnduniɑ kpuro
bba	I wɛ̃ro tɔ̃ɔ wɛ̃rɑruɡiru sɔɔ, kpɑ i tu ɡɑrisi te
bba	Wi u tɔnu so u ɡo, bɑ koo yɛ̃ron tii ɡowɑ.

bba	Wunɛ Mɔwisi, kɑɑ mɑn susimɑ wunɛ turo. Be bɑ kɑ nun
bba	yɔɔmɑ bu yɔ̃ro mi bɑ wɑ̃ɑ mi. Tɔn be bɑ mɑɑ tie, bu
bba	Sumi yi sɔɔrɑ dɑ̃ɑ pɔɔsi yi, yi ko n dɑ n wɑ̃ɑ. Bɑ
bba	Kpɑ ɑ mɑɑ bekunu wɔkurɑ tiɑ wesi kɑ boo sɑnsu ni bɑ
bba	koo kuu bekuruɡii te wukiri.

bba	win senɔ, niyɑ nu koo sɔ̃ɔsi mɑ kɑ Isirelibɑn yĩsinɑ u

bba	A bu sokoto kpirinu kuo kpɑ bu ku kɑ ben tereru wɑn sɔ̃.
bba	Kɑɑ ye kpuro kowɑ kɑ wɛ̃ɛ dɑmɡii.

bba	ɡɑri kpɑ ɑ de ben bɑɑwure u ɡobi ɡɛɛ wɛ̃ u kɑ win

bba	kpee bɛsi yiru ye nɛni yèn beri yiru yiru kpuro bɑ yoruɑ.
bba	Ù n duɑ mi, sɑɑ yerɑ ɡuru wii wuro te, tɑ rɑ sɑrɑmɛ
bba	tu yɔ̃rɑ kuu ten kɔnnɔwɔ kpɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u kɑ nùn
bba	Sɔrɔkudo i ko bɛɛn bii tɔn durɔbu kurɔbu suɑ ben bii
bba	wɔndiɑbɑ sɔɔ, kpɑ kurɔ be, bu de bɛɛn bii be, bu nɛn
bba	sɑ̃ɑru deri bu tɔn ben bũnu sɑ̃.
bba	kɑ kpee ɡobiɡinu nìn nɔni sɑ̃ɑ bɛrɔ wuru ni bɑ koo
bba	doke yɑbe tɑrɑkpe ɡe sɔɔ, kɑ ni bɑ koo doke bɔɔ bɑrɑ
bba	Mɑ tɔn be bɑ sɔmbu te mɔ̀ mi, ben bɑɑwure u ɡinɑ win
bba	Mɑ bɑ beku kɑreru kuɑ kɑ wɛ̃ɛ dɑmɡii kɑ wɛ̃ɛ yi
bba	bɑ wɔ̃kuɑ kɑ burɑ kɑ mɑɑ ɡɑɑdurɑ, kɑ wɛ̃ɛ
bba	wunɔmɡii. Mɑ bɑ wɔllun kɔ̃sobun weenɑsibu kuɑ beku te
bba	Mɑ bɑ dɑ̃ɑ pɔɔsi yi kuɑ kɑ ɑkɑsiɑn dɑ̃ɑ bɑ yi
bba	Sii ɡɑn niyɑ bɑ kɑ kuu ten kɔnnɔn dɑ̃ɑ bɛsi
bba	sinumɡiin yɔ̃rɑtii kuɑ kɑ yɑ̃ku yee te, kɑ ten
bba	kɔkɔsɔ ye, kɑ ten dendi yɑ̃nu.
bba	Bɑ mɑɑ sɛ̃kɑtiɑ ye wesɑ kɑ wɛ̃ɛ dɑmɡii bɑ burɑru
bba	koosi kɑ wɛ̃ɛ yi bɑ wɔ̃kuɑ kɑ burɑ kɑ mɑɑ
bba	ɡɑɑdurɑ kɑ wɛ̃ɛ wunɔmɡii. Mɛyɑ bɑ ye kpuro kuɑ
bba	nɡe mɛ Yinni Gusunɔ u Mɔwisi sɔ̃ɔwɑ.
bba	Yen biru kɑɑ kɑ Aroni kɑ win bibu nɑ kuu ten kɔnnɔwɔ,
bba	kpɑ ɑ bu wobure kɑ nim dirum.
bba	U koo win nɔmɑ sɔndiwɑ kɛtɛ yen wiru wɔllɔ ye nɛ
bba	Gusunɔ nɑ wurɑ yu kɑ win durum wukiri.
bba	Goo ù n siɑrɑbun yɑ̃kuru mɔ̀ Yinni Gusunɔn mi kɑ kɛtɛ
bba	kinɛru, ǹ kun mɛ kɑ kɛtɛ niɑ, yen ye u wɑ kpurowɑ u
bba	koo kɑ nɑ, yɑ kun ɡesi ɑlebu mɔ.
bba	Adɑmɑ bɑ̀ n tubɑ mɑ bɑ torɑwɑ mi, bɑ koo nɑɑ kinɛ
bba	kpɛmbu ɡowɑ bu kɑ ben torɑ ten suuru kɑnɑ. Bɑ koo kɑ
bba	nɑɑ kinɛ te dɑwɑ Yinni Gusunɔn kurun kɔnnɔwɔ.
bba	Kpɑ u ɡen yɛm dɛkɑ u yɛ̃ke yɑ̃ku yerun nɔɔ bɔkɑɔ,
bba	mɛ mu tie kpɑ u wisi ten temɔ. Yɑ ko n sɑ̃ɑwɑ torɑrun
bba	Aronin bii tɔn durɔ bɑɑwurewɑ u koo dĩɑ ni di. Yeni yɑ
bba	ko n sɑ̃ɑwɑ woodɑ win bibun bweseru sɔɔ sere kɑ
bba	bɑɑdommɑɔ. Tɔn tuko wi u koo nu bɑbɑ kpuro u koo ɡbiwɑ.
bba	Adɑmɑ ɡoo ù n yɑ̃kuru kuɑ u kɑ win nɔɔ mwɛɛru yibiɑ
bba	ǹ kun mɛ win tii ù n ɡɔ̃ru doke u kɑ nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔ
bba	kɛ̃ru wɛ̃, u koo kpĩ u ten yɑɑn sukum di yen tɔ̃ɔ te,
bba	kpɑ u sukum yi sere sisiru.
bba	Mɑ u bɔɔ bɑrɑ ye sɔndi win tororu wɔllɔ. Mɑ u urimu kɑ
bba	tumimu doke bɔɔ bɑrɑ yen sɔɔwɔ.
bba	U Aroni sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɑ nɑɑ kinɛ kpɛndu suo ɑ kɑ
bba	yɑ̃kuru ko wunɛn torɑrun sɔ̃, kpɑ ɑ yɑ̃ɑ kinɛru
bba	kɑsu ɑ kɑ yɑ̃ku dɔ̃ɔ mwɑɑrɑruɡiru ko. A ǹ kɑɑ de
bba	yen ɡɑɑ yɑ n ɑlebu mɔ. Kpɑ ɑ kɑ ye kpuro Yinni Gusunɔ
bba	Mɑ bɑ nɑ bɑ ɡoo ni suɑ kɑ nin tɑkobɑ sɑnnu bɑ kɑ dɑ
bba	sɑnsɑnin biruɔ nɡe mɛ Mɔwisi u ɡeruɑ.
bba	kɑ tɑɑtɑɑnu kɑ booro kɑ sere si su kɑ su weenɛ kɑ
bba	kɑsɑ kɑ si su kɑ ye weenɛ,
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u Mɔwisi woodɑ wɛ̃ u nɛɛ,
bba	Mɔsi te, tɑ̀ n ɡɔnɑ yɑbi, yɑ̃ku kowo u koo nùn
bba	ɡɑrisiwɑ disiɡii domi bɑrɑ disiɡirɑ tɑ nùn deemɑ.
bba	u koo de bu nu teɑwɑ kpɑ bu mɑɑ nu diru kɛnusi sɔ̃ɔ
bba	Yen biru u koo yɑ̃ɑ te sɑkɑ kpɑ u ten yɛm suɑ u tɛɛni
bba	wi u rɑɑ bɑrɑ disiɡiru mɔn soo nɔm ɡeuɡuuɔ kɑ win
bba	nɔm ɡeun niki biɑ bɑkɑɔ kɑ sere mɑɑ win nɔɔ nɔm
bba	55-56 kɑ mɔsiru kɑ debu kɑ disi ɡɔmi yi yi rɑ kpi yɑ̃nu
bba	Yen sɔ̃ɔ nɔɔbɑ itɑse sɔɔrɑ u koo kpɑrukonu yiru ǹ
bba	kun mɛ totobɛrɛnu yiru kɑsu kpɑ u kɑ yɑ̃ku kowo dɑɑwɑ
bba	Wi u boo ɡe ɡirɑ u kɑ dɑ ɡbɑburɔ u koo win yɑ̃nu
bba	teɑwɑ kpɑ u wobure u sere du sɑnsɑniɔ.
bba	Ǹ n mɛn nɑ, i nɛn ɡere kɑ nɛn woodɑbɑ mɛm nɔɔwɔ.
bba	Wi u ye mɛm nɔɔwɑ u ko n wɑ̃ɑwɑ yen sɔ̃. Nɛ Yinni
bba	Ì n nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔ siɑrɑbun yɑ̃kuru kuɑmmɛ, i tu
bba	koowo nɡe mɛ tɑ koo kɑ mɑn wɛ̃re.
bba	I ku murɑfitiru ko siribu sɔɔ, kɑ ɡɑ̃ɑ yĩirubu sɔɔ,
bba	kɑ kilobɑ sɔɔ kɑ sɑkɑkunu sɔɔ.
bba	Nɛnɑ Gusunɔ bɛɛn Yinni nɛ wi nɑ bɛɛ wunɑ sɑɑ bwese
bba	Ben bweseru sɔɔ, ɡoo ù n nu susi, mɑ u disi ɡɛɛ mɔ, bɑ
bba	koo yɛ̃ro yɑrɑwɑ nɛn sɔmburun di.
bba	Nɛnɑ nɑ bɛɛ yɑrɑ sɑɑ Eɡibitin di nɑ n kɑ sɑ̃ɑ
bba	33-34 Yinni Gusunɔ u Isirelibɑ sɔ̃ɔwɑ sɑɑ Mɔwisin
bba	nɔɔn di u nɛɛ, sɑɑ wɔ̃ɔn suru nɔɔbɑ yirusen sɔ̃ɔ
bba	wɔkurɑ nɔɔbun di, i ko i Kunun tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑru diwɑ
bba	sɔ̃ɔ nɔɔbɑ yiru i kɑ nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔ sɑ̃.
bba	Wi u yɑɑ sɑberu ɡo, u koo ten kɔsire wɛ̃wɑ. Wi u mɑɑ
bba	tɔnu ɡo, bɑ koo mɑɑ yɛ̃ro ɡowɑ.
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u nɛɛ, ɡoo ù n win diru dɔrɑ te tɑ wɑ̃ɑ
bba	wuu ɡbɑ̃rɑruɡuu sɔɔ, wɔ̃ɔ tiɑ u mɔ u kɑ tu yɑkiɑ.
bba	kon de ɡurɑ yu nɛ yen sɑɑ sɔɔ kpɑ tem mu dĩɑnu wɛ̃
bba	Kon de bu bɛɛ tɑbu wɔri kpɑ i yɑrinɑ i dɑ tem tukumɔ.
bba	Kpɑ bɛɛn wusu su ko bɑnsu.
bba	Ù n ɡbee te Yinni Gusunɔ wɛ̃ yɑkiɑbun tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑrun
bba	biru, yɑ̃ku kowo u koo ten ɡobi kɑwɑwɑ. U koo wɔ̃ɔ si
bba	su tie sere yɑkiɑbun tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑru tu kɑ turin ɡobi
bba	kɑ Akiesɛɛ, Amisɑdɑin bii, Dɑnun bweseru sɔɔ,
bba	Adɑmɑ Lefibɑ bɑ koo ben sɑnsɑni ɡirɑwɑ bu kɑ kuu te
bba	sikerenɑ mi woodɑn kpɑkororɑ wɑ̃ɑ. Nɡe mɛyɑ bɑ koo
bba	kɑ tu kɔ̃su. Sɑɑ ye sɔɔ, Isirelibɑ bɑǹ mɑɑ wɑsi bu
bba	tu susi n sere kɑ bu mɔru ko.
bba	Be kpuro kɑ Efɑrɑimun tɑbu kowobun ɡeerɑ kuɑwɑ tɔmbu
bba	nɔrɔbun subɑ wunɔbu kɑ nɔɔbɑ itɑ kɑ wunɔbu (108.100).
bba	Mɑ Mɔwisi u bu ɡɑrɑ nɡe mɛ Yinni Gusunɔ u ɡeruɑ.
bba	Bɑ̀ n kĩ bu Isirelibɑn bii ɡbiikobu ɡoobu kɑ wɑtɑ kɑ
bba	wɔkurɑ itɑ (273) be bɑ Lefibɑ dɑbiru kere mi yɑkiɑ,
bba	kɑ ten yɑɑrɑn bekɑ kɑ yen kɔnnɔn beku kɑreru kɑ ten
bba	wɛ̃ɛ kɑ ten sɔm yɑ̃ɑ ni nu tie. Ye kpuron sɔmburɑ bɑ
bba	U koo de kurɔ wi, u yɔ̃rɑ Yinni Gusunɔn wuswɑɑɔ kpɑ u
bba	nùn win yɑsɑ potɑ, kpɑ u kɛ̃ɛ te sɔndi kurɔ win
bba	nɔmɑɔ. Sɑɑ ye sɔɔ, yɑ̃ku kowon tii u ko n nim sosurɑm
bba	nɛni mɛ mu kɑ bɔ̃ri nɑɑmɔ,
bba	Kpɑ u mɑɑ siɑrɑbun yɑ̃kunu ko kɑ yɑ̃ɑ kinɛ te, kɑ
bba	pɛ̃ɛ ye yɑ wɑ̃ɑ bire te sɔɔ, ye bɑǹ seeyɑtiɑ doke,
bba	Tɔ̃ru nnɛse Elisuri, Sedeurin bii, Rubɛnin bweseru sɔɔ, u
bba	nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔn wuswɑɑɔ, kpɑ Isirelibɑ bu ben nɔmɑ
bba	sɔndi Lefi ben wiru wɔllɔ.
bba	Sɔɔ ɡoo ù n wɑ̃ɑ bɛɛn suunu sɔɔ, u tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑ te
bba	dimɔ, u koo tu diwɑ nɡe mɛ nɑ ten woodɑ yi. Bɛɛ kɑ
bba	sɔbu, woodɑ tiɑ yerɑ nɑ bɛɛ wɛ̃ɛmɔ.
bba	Mɔwisi u Hobɑbu win kurɔn sesu, Rewɛli Mɑdiɑnin bii
bba	sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, sɑ dɔɔwɑ tem mi Yinni Gusunɔ u sun
bba	nɔɔ mwɛɛru kuɑ u sun wɛ̃. A nɑ ɑ kɑ sun dɑ, kpɑ su
bba	kɑ nun durom mɛ bɔnu ko, mɛ Yinni Gusunɔ u bɛsɛ
bba	Isirelibɑ nɔɔ mwɛɛru kuɑ.
bba	Mɑ Mɔwisi u yɑrɑ u dɑ u Yinni Gusunɔn ɡɑri yi tɔn be
bba	sɔ̃ɔwɑ. U Isirelibɑn ɡuro ɡurobu wɑtɑ kɑ wɔkuru
bba	mɛnnɑ. Mɑ u derɑ bɑ sinɑ bɑ kɑ kuu te sikerenɑ.
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u Mɔwisi sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ,
bba	Mɑ Amɑlɛkibɑ bɑ wɑ̃ɑ mɛn sɔ̃ɔ yɛ̃sɑn nɔm dwɑru
bba	ɡiɑ. Mɑ Hɛtibɑ kɑ Yebusibɑ kɑ Amɔrebɑ bɑ wɑ̃ɑ
bba	ɡuunun berɑ ɡiɑ. Kɑnɑnibɑ bɑ mɑɑ wɑ̃ɑ nim wɔ̃ku
bba	ɡe bɑ mɔ̀ Mɛditerɑnɛn bɔkuɔ, kɑ sere Yuudɛnin
bba	nɑ nuɑ Isirelibɑ bɑ mɑn wɔkisimɔ. Sere sɑɑ yerɑ̀ bɑ
bba	Yɑ̃kuru bɑɑterewɑ i ko i n dɑ kue mɛ, nɡe mɛ ten woodɑ
bba	be kpurowɑ bɑ Mɔwisi seesi, kɑ sere mɑɑ tɔmbu ɡoobu kɑ
bba	weerɑɑkuru (250) ɡɑbu be bɑ sɑ̃ɑ Isirelibɑn wiruɡii be
bba	Adɑmɑ Yinni Gusunɔ ù n ɡɑ̃ɑ nɑnumɡinu kuɑ, u derɑ
bba	tem mu nɔɔ bɑɑrɑ mu bu mwɛ kɑ ye bɑ mɔ kpuro, kpɑ bu
bba	dɑ ɡɔribun wɑ̃ɑ yerɔ, sɑɑ yerɑ, i ko i ɡiɑ mɑ tɔn
bba	be, bɑ Yinni Gusunɔ ɡɛmɑwɑ.
bba	Mɑ Mɔwisi u dɛki yi ɡurɑ Yinni Gusunɔn wuswɑɑn di, u kɑ
bba	dɑ Isirelibɑ kpuron wuswɑɑɔ bu kɑ wɑ kpɑ ben bɑɑwure u
bba	ɑ Lefibɑ sɔ̃ɔwɔ ɑ nɛɛ, Isirelibɑn ye bɑ wɑ kpuron
bba	wɔkuru bɑɑtere sɔɔ, yen tiɑ tiɑ ye bɑ rɑ mɑn wɛ̃,
bba	Lefi be, bɑ̀ n ye mwɑ yɑ kuɑ beɡiɑ, ben tii bu mɑɑ
bba	wɔkuru bɑɑtere sɔɔ tiɑ wunɔ nɛn sɔ̃.
bba	Sɑɑ ye sɔɔrɑ Isirelibɑ bɑ nim biɑ mɑ bɑ Mɔwisi kɑ
bba	Mɑ u Isirelibɑn ɡɑri yi wurɑ u bu Kɑnɑni be nɔmu
bba	bɛriɑ. Mɑ bɑ Kɑnɑni be, kɑ ben wusu kpeerɑsiɑ. Yerɑ
bba	bɑ yɑm mi yĩsiru kɑ̃ Hɔɔmɑ. Yen tubusiɑnɑ bɑnsu.
bba	I nɑ i Sihonin wuu bɑni i ɡu ɡbɑ̃rɑru toosi.
bba	Gusunɔ u Bɑlɑmu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɑ ku dɑ. A ku tɔn be
bba	bɔ̃rusi domi nɑ bu domɑru kuɑ.
bba	Yerɑ Bɑlɑki u kɛtɛbɑ kɑ yɑ̃ɑnu ɡo u kɑ yɑ̃kuru
bba	Mɑ u ɡɑri ɡerubu wɔri u nɛɛ,
bba	Nɑ rɑ Yinni Gusunɔn nɔɔ nɔ.
bba	Mɑ wɔndiɑ be, bɑ derɑ Isireli be, bɑ ben bũu sɑ̃ɑru
bba	wɔri, bɑ kɑ bu di, bɑ kɑ bu nɔrɑ. Mɑ bɑ ben bũnu
bba	Be bɑ sɑ̃ɑ Simɛɔn bwese kɛri, berɑ mi. Ben ɡeerɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ tɔmbu nɔrɔbun subɑ yɛndɑ yiru kɑ tɔmbu ɡoobu
bba	Asɛɛ u bii tɔn kurɔ mɔ wi bɑ sokumɔ Serɑki.
bba	Win tundo ù kun mɑɑ mɑɑbu kɑ wɔnɔbu mɔ, win mɛro bisi
bba	wi u fɛ̃ɛ fɛ̃ɛ bo wiyɑ u koo win ɑrumɑni tubi di. Yeni
bba	yɑ ko n sɑ̃ɑwɑ woodɑ Isirelibɑ sɔɔ nɡe mɛ nɛ, Yinni
bba	Tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑ ten tɔ̃ɔ ɡbiikiru sɔɔ, i ko i bɛɛn sɔmɑ
bba	deriwɑ, kpɑ i mɛnnɑ i nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔ sɑ̃.
bba	17-34 Tɔ̃ɔ bɑɑteren yɑ̃ku ni bɑɑsi, i ko i mɑɑ
bba	yɑ̃kunu ko kɑ yɑɑ sɑbe ni nuǹ ɑlebu ɡɑɑ mɔ kɑ
bba	mɑɑ som mɛ bɑ burinɑ kɑ ɡum, nɡe mɛ i rɑ ko sɑɑ
bba	tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑ ten sɔ̃ɔ yirusen di n kɑ ɡirɑri ten sɔ̃ɔ
bba	nɔɔbɑ yiruse. Nɡe mɛniwɑ i ko i yɑ̃ku ni koosinɑ.
bba	ɑ doo ɑ Mɑdiɑnibɑ mɔru kɔsiɑ kɔ̃sɑ ye bɑ Isirelibɑ
bba	kuɑn sɔ̃. Yen biruwɑ kon de ɑ kpunɑ ɑ ɡbi ɑ wunɛn
bba	Arumɑni ye bɑ ɡurɑ kpuro, yen ɡeeru wee. Yɑ̃ɑnu kɑ
bba	bonun ɡeerɑ sɑ̃ɑ nɔrɔbun subɑ nɑtɑ kɑ wɑtɑ kɑ
bba	Ye bɑ ɡɔsirɑmɑ, mɑ bɑ beɡibu Isirelibɑ mwiɑ
bba	kpɑnɑsiɑ bu ku kɑ dɑ tem mɛ Yinni Gusunɔ u bu wɛ̃ sɔɔ.
bba	Mɑkiri Mɑnɑsen biin sikɑdominu, beyɑ bɑ Gɑlɑdin tem
bba	wɔri bɑ Amɔrebɑ ɡirɑ tem mɛn di mɑ bɑ mu mwɑ.
bba	Sɑɑ min diyɑ bɑ dɑ bɑ ben sɑnsɑni ɡirɑ Mitikɑɔ.
bba	Sɔ̃ɔ yɛ̃sɑn nɔm dwɑru ɡiɑ mu koo nɔɔ yɔ̃rɑwɑ
bba	berɑ mi bɑ mɔ̀ Siniɔ mi tem mu sɑɑrɑm sɑ̃ɑ kpɑ ɡu
bba	mɑɑ dɑ Mɔɑbun tem bɔkuɔ. Nɔɔ ɡe, ɡɑ koo torewɑ nim
bba	wɔ̃ku bɔruɡuun bɔkuɔ, sɔ̃ɔ yɑri yeru ɡiɑ.
bba	kpɑ nin dɛ̃ɛbu bu n sɑ̃ɑ ɡɔm soonu nɔrɔbun subɑ yiru
bba	(2.000) sɔ̃ɔ yɑri yeru ɡiɑ, kɑ sɔ̃ɔ duu yeru ɡiɑ,
bba	kɑ sɔ̃ɔ yɛ̃sɑn nɔm dwɑru ɡiɑ, kɑ mɑɑ nɔm ɡeu
bba	ɡiɑ, kpɑ wuu ɡɑ n wɑ̃ɑ suunu sɔɔ. Nɡe mɛyɑ ben
bba	kpɑrɑ yee ni, nu ko n sɑ̃ɑ wuu bɑɑɡere sɔɔ.
bba	Mɑ Mɔwisi u Isirelibɑ sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, Yosɛfun bweserun
bba	Bɛɛn ɡɑri yi, yi mɑn wɛ̃re, mɑ nɑ tɔmbu wɔkurɑ yiru
bba	ɡɔsɑ bɛɛn bwese kɛrɑ bɑɑyere sɔɔ tiɑ tiɑ.
bba	Domi Gusunɔ bɛsɛn Yinni u bɛsɛn sɔmɑ kpuro domɑru kuɑ
bba	mɑ u sun kɔ̃su sɑnɑm mɛ sɑ ɡbɑbu bɑkɑ te
bba	bukiɑnɑmɔ. U wɑ̃ɑ kɑ bɛsɛ sere n kɑ kuɑ ɡisɔ
bba	wɔ̃ɔ weeru. Sɑ ǹ ɡɑ̃ɑnu bie.
bba	Adɑmɑ sɑ ǹ Amɔnibɑn tem bɑbe kɑ tem mɛ mu wɑ̃ɑ
bba	Yɑbɔkun dɑɑrun ɡoorɔ kɑ wuu si su wɑ̃ɑ ɡuunɔ kɑ
bba	sere mi Gusunɔ bɛsɛn Yinni u sun yinɑri su wɔri.
bba	Tɛ̃, bɛɛ Isirelibɑ, i yiirebu kɑ woodɑbɑ swɑɑ dɑkio
bba	be nɑ bɛɛ wɛ̃ɛmɔ. I ye mɛm nɔɔwɔ kpɑ i wɑ i n
bba	wɑ̃ɑ, kpɑ i du tem mɛ sɔɔ, mɛ Gusunɔ bɛsɛn
bba	bɑɑbɑbɑn Yinni u bɛɛ wɛ̃.
bba	Domi u sɑ̃ɑwɑ wɔnwɔnduɡii wi u kun bɛɛ derimɔ. U ǹ
bba	bɛɛ kpeerɑsiɑmɔ. U ǹ mɑɑ duɑrimɔ ɑrukɑwɑni ye u
bba	kɑ bɛɛn bɑɑbɑbɑ bɔkuɑ kɑ bɔ̃ri.
bba	Sɔ̃ɔ nɔɔbɑ tiɑ sɔɔrɑ sɑ ko n dɑ bɛsɛn sɔmɑ kpuro
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ Gusunɔ bɛsɛn Yinni u koo bɛɛ kpɑrɑ u kɑ dɑ
bba	tem mɛ u koo bɛɛ wɛ̃ sɔɔ, nɡe mɛ u bɛsɛn bɑɑbɑbɑ,
bba	Aburɑhɑmu kɑ Isɑki kɑ Yɑkɔbu nɔɔ mwɛɛru kuɑ, i ko i
bba	wuu bɑkɑsu kɑ wuu burɔsu wɑ si i ǹ bɑnɛ,
bba	I ko i bwesenu kpuro kpeerɑsiɑwɑ mɑm mɑm ni Yinni Gusunɔ u
bba	bɛɛ nɔmu bɛriɑ. I ku rɑ nin wɔnwɔndu ko, i ku rɑ mɑɑ
bba	nin bũnu sɑ̃. Domi bũu ni, nu ko n sɑ̃ɑwɑ yinɑ bɛɛn
bba	Bɛɛ Isirelibɑ, i swɑɑ dɑkio i nɔ. Wee ɡisɔ, i ko i
bba	Yuudɛni tɔburɑ kpɑ i bwese bɑkɑnu ɡirɑ ni nu bɛɛ dɑm
bba	kere, kpɑ i ben wuu bɑkɑsu mwɑ si bɑ ɡbɑ̃rɑnu toosi nu
bba	Mɑ nɑ kpɑkoro te kuɑ kɑ ɑkɑsiɑn dɑ̃ɑ. Nɑ kpee bɛsi
bba	yiru ye dɑ̃kɑ yi kɑ yiɔnɔ weenɛ. Mɑ nɑ yɔɔwɑ ɡuu
bba	ten wɔllɔ nɑ kpee bɛsi yi nɛni.
bba	Tem mɛni, mu sɑ̃ɑwɑ tem ɡuunuɡim kɑ wɔwiɡim mɛ̀
bba	Geemɑ, i ǹ ɡinɑ turɑ tem mɛ sɔɔ, mɛ Gusunɔ bɛsɛn
bba	Yinni u koo bɛɛ wɛ̃ kpɑ i n kɑ wɑ̃ɑru dimɔ bɔri
bba	I ku rɑ yɛ̃ro swɑɑ dɑki i win ɡɑri ɡem mwɑ. I ku rɑ
bba	mɑɑ win wɔnwɔndu ko i sere nùn biru wukiri.
bba	Wɔ̃ɔ bɑɑɡere, bɛɛn ɡbeɑn dĩɑnu sɔɔ, wɔkuru
bba	bɑɑteren wɔllɔ tiɑ tiɑwɑ i ko i n dɑ wunɛ,
bba	Suru wi bɑ mɔ̀ Abibu sɔɔ, i ku rɑ duɑri i Gɔɔ
bba	sɑrɑribun tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑru di Gusunɔ bɛsɛn Yinnin sɔ̃.
bba	Domi suru wi sɔɔrɑ u bɛɛ yɑrɑ Eɡibitin di wɔ̃kuru.
bba	I ko i kowɑ dee dee ye bɑ bɛɛ sɔ̃ɔwɑ sɑ̃ɑ yee ten min
bba	di tè Yinni Gusunɔ u tii ɡɔsiɑ.
bba	Adɑmɑ sɔmɔ wi, ù n ɡɑri ɡɛɛ sosi kɑ Yinni Gusunɔn
bba	yĩsiru ye u ǹ nùn yiire u ɡere ǹ kun mɛ ù n ɡɑri
bba	ɡeruɑ kɑ bũnun yĩsiru, bɑ koo nùn ɡowɑ.
bba	Bɑ̀ n ɡɑri yi ɡeruɑ bɑ kpɑ, kpɑ bu bu tɑbu sinɑmbu
bba	sɑɑ ye sɔɔ, win tundo kɑ win mɛro bɑ koo nùn mwɑwɑ bu
bba	kɑ nɑ wuun ɡuro ɡurobun mi,
bba	I ku wɔndiɑ wi ɡɑ̃ɑnu kuɑ. U ǹ torɑru ɡɑru kue te
bba	tɑ weenɛ bu kɑ nùn ɡo. N sɑ̃ɑwɑ nɡe durɔ ɡoo wi u
bba	Goo ù n kurɔ suɑ mɑ u kurɔ wi ɡɑ̃ɑnu wɑɑsi ye yɑ ǹ
bba	kɑ nùn nɑɑwɛ, mɑ u kurɔ wi yinɑnɑɑn tireru yoruɑ u
bba	nùn nɔmu bɛriɑ, mɑ u nùn ɡirɑ win yɛnun di u doonɑ,
bba	Kpɑ bu win bweseru yĩsiru kɛ̃ Isirelibɑ sɔɔ bu nɛɛ,
bba	wìn bɑrɑ nɔɔ bɑ wunɑn bweseru.
bba	Mɔwisi kɑ Isirelibɑn ɡuro ɡurobu bɑ tɔmbu sɔ̃ɔwɑ bɑ
bba	nɛɛ, i woodɑ be kpuro mɛm nɔɔwɔ be Mɔwisi u bɛɛ
bba	U koo de i dɑ̃ɑ bii dɑbinu wɑ i birenu yibiɑ kpɑ u de i n
bba	som mɔ mu n kpɑ̃ i kɑ pɛ̃ɛ ko.
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u koo de i bosu wɑ si i ǹ bɛkurɑmɔ. Su ko n
bba	wɑ̃ɑwɑ bɛɛn dũunɔ kɑ bɛɛn tɑɑnɔ kpɑ su yɛ̃bi
bba	bɛɛn wɑsi kpuro sɔɔ sɑɑ bɛɛn wirun di sere kɑ bɛɛn
bba	Bwese ni sɔɔ, i ǹ bɔri yɛndu wɑsi. Mɛyɑ i ǹ sinɑmɔ
bba	yɑm tem. Yinni Gusunɔ u koo de i burisinɑ kpɑ i n nuki
bba	Ye yɑ beruɑ, Yinni Gusunɔ turowɑ u ye yɛ̃. Adɑmɑ
bba	bɛsɛɡiɑ ye u sun sɔ̃ɔsi bɛsɛ kɑ bɛsɛn bibun bweseru
bba	kpɑ su win woodɑ ye mɛm nɔɔwɑ.
bba	U bu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, wɔ̃ɔ nɔɔbɑ yiru bɑɑyere yè
bba	sɔɔ bɑ rɑ be bɑ dibu nɛni kɑre, Kunun tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑrun
bba	Mɑ u bu ɡberun dĩɑnu diisiɑ.
bba	Ben yibɛrɛ be, bɑ sɑnkirewɑ nɡe Sodomu kɑ Gomɔrɑɡibu.
bba	U rɑ tɔmbu kpuro kɔ̃su be bɑ sɑ̃ɑ wiɡibu,
bba	bɛɛ Isirelibɑ, i n yɛ̃ mɑ Yinni ɡoo sɑri nɡe Gusunɔ.
bba	Mɔwisi, Yinni Gusunɔn sɔm kowon ɡɔɔn biru, Yinni Gusunɔ u
bba	kɑ Yosue, Mɔwisin ɑsɑkpɔ ɡbiikoo wi u sɑ̃ɑ Nunin bii
bba	N deemɑ Rɑhɑbun diru tɑ ɡirɑriwɑ wuun ɡbɑ̃rɑru sɔɔ,
bba	mɑ u bu sɑrɑsiɑ wuun biruɔ win fɛnɛntin di kɑ wɛ̃ɛ
bba	Mɑ Yosue u durɔbu wɔkurɑ yiru ye sokɑ be u ɡɔsɑ
bba	Isirelibɑ bɑ sinɑ ben sɑnsɑniɔ Giliɡɑli mi, ye yɑ
bba	wɑ̃ɑ wɔwɑɔ Yerikon bɔkuɔ. Mɑ bɑ Gɔɔ sɑrɑribun
bba	tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑru di surun sɔ̃ɔ wɔkurɑ nnɛsen yokɑ.
bba	Yen biruwɑ bɑ wuu ɡe dɔ̃ɔ sɔkɑ kɑ bɑɑyere kpuro ye
bba	yɑ wɑ̃ɑ wuu ɡe sɔɔ mɑ n kun mɔ ye n sɑ̃ɑ sii ɡeesu,
bba	kɑ wurɑ, kɑ sii ɡɑndu kɑ sere sii wɔ̃kusu. Yerɑ bɑ
bba	doke Yinni Gusunɔn sɑ̃ɑ yerun ɑrumɑnin beru yerɔ.
bba	Ye sɑ tɑbu di sɑ mwɑ sɔɔ, nɑ yɑbe burɑru ɡɑru wɑ te
bba	bɑ kuɑ Bɑbiloniɔ kɑ sii ɡeesun ɡobi ɡoobu (200) kɑ
bba	wurɑ dɛkɑ yèn bunum kɑ kilon bɔnu nɛ. Nɑ ye binɛ kuɑ
bba	mɑ nɑ suɑ nɑ sikuɑ nɛn kurɔ, sii ɡee siyɑ su wɑ̃ɑ
bba	Ye Isirelibɑ bɑ ben yibɛrɛ be mwɑ bɑ ɡo ɡo ɡbɑburu mi,
bba	mi bɑ bu nɑɑ swĩi, yerɑ bɑ mɑɑ ɡɔsirɑmɑ Ayiɔ bɑ
bba	Tilɑsiwɑ su kɑ bu deri. Mɑ n kun mɛ, sɑ ko Yinni Gusunɔn
bba	Mɑ Yosuen tɔmbu bɑ wurɑmɑ kɑ bɔri yɛndu win mi
bba	Mɑkedɑɔ. Tem mɛ sɔɔ, ɡoo kun mɑɑ kɑ̃kɑ u ben
bba	Sɑɑ yerɑ Yosue kɑ win tɑbu kowobu bɑ dɑ bɑ tɔn be wɔri
bba	subɑru sɔɔ Mɛromun dɑɑru mi.
bba	kɑ sere Sihoni Amɔreɡii wi u rɑɑ bɑndu dii Hɛsiboniɔn
bba	wuu si su wɑ̃ɑ bɑtumɑ sɔɔ. N deemɑ Mɔwisi u sunɔ wi
bba	kɑmiɑ, kɑ Mɑdiɑnibɑn sinɑmbu. Beyɑ Efi kɑ Rekɛmu kɑ
bba	Suri kɑ Huri kɑ Rebɑ. Be kpurowɑ bɑ rɑɑ Sihoni sɑ̃ɑmɔ.
bba	mɑ tɑ dɑ ɡunɡuu te bɑ mɔ̀ Akɑrɑbimuɔ kɑ Siniɔ sere
bba	kɑ Kɑdɛsi Bɑɑnɛɑɔ. Sɑɑ mɑɑ min di, tɑ dɑ
bba	Hɛsironiɔ kɑ Adɑriɔ sere kɑ Kɑɑkɑɑɔ.
bba	kɑ Sikilɑɡi, kɑ Mɑdimɑnɑ, kɑ Sɑnsɑnɑ,
bba	Wuu si su wɑ̃ɑ berɑ mi ɡɑ̃ɑnu ku rɑ kpi, siyɑ Bɛti
bba	Arɑbɑ, kɑ Midini, kɑ Sekɑkɑ,
bba	Mɑ Yosue u Efɑrɑimun bwese kɛrɑ ye kɑ Mɑnɑsen bwese
bba	kɛrɑn sukum mɛ sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, i dɑbi, i mɑɑ dɑm mɔ.
bba	Yen sɔ̃, n ǹ tem bɛsi tiɑ tɔnɑ mu ko n sɑ̃ɑ bɛɛɡim.
bba	kɑ Selɑ, kɑ Elɛfu, kɑ Yebusi ye bɑ mɑɑ mɔ̀
bba	Yerusɑlɛmu, kɑ Gibeɑ kɑ Kiriɑti. Si kpuro su sɑ̃ɑwɑ
bba	wusu wɔkurɑ nnɛ, ɡen bɑɑɡere kɑ ɡen bɑru kpɑɑnu.
bba	Min di tɑ mɑɑ dɑ Rɑmɑ ɡiɑ kɑ sere Tiriɔ, wuu ɡe bɑ
bba	ɡbɑ̃rɑru koosi, sere n kɑ ɡirɑri Hosɑɔ mɑ tɑ yɔ̃rɑ
bba	nim wɔ̃ku ɡe bɑ mɔ̀ Mɛditerɑnɛɔ, Akisibun berɑɔ.
bba	Yuudɛnin ɡuru ɡiɔ bɑ mɑɑ Besɛɛ ɡɔsɑ Yerikon sɔ̃ɔ
bba	yɑri yeru ɡiɑ bɑtumɑɔ mi ɡɑ̃ɑnu ku rɑ kpi,
bba	Rubɛnibɑn tem sɔɔ, kɑ Rɑmɔti ye yɑ wɑ̃ɑ Gɑlɑdiɔ,
bba	Gɑdibɑn tem sɔɔ, kɑ Golɑni ye yɑ wɑ̃ɑ Bɑsɑniɔ
bba	Asɛɛbɑn tem sɔɔ, bɑ bu Mikɑli kɑ Abudoni kɑ Hɛlikɑti
bba	I yɑɑyo sɑnɑm mɛ Akɑni wi u wɑ̃ɑ Serɑkin bweseru sɔɔ
bba	u torɑ ye u kɑ ɑrumɑni suɑ ye bɑ nɛɛ, ɡoo u ku suɑ.
bba	Isirelibɑ kpurowɑ Gusunɔ u seesi. Domi n ǹ Akɑni tɔnɑ u
bba	ɡu dɔmɑ te, torɑ ten sɔ̃.
bba	Mɛyɑ i n mɑɑ yɛ̃ nɡe mɛ u nɔɔ mwɛɛ ɡee ni yibiɑ
bba	mi, mɛyɑ u koo mɑɑ kɔ̃sɑ ye u ɡeruɑ kpuro ko. U koo
bba	bɛɛ ɡo mɑm mɑm tem durom mɛ sɔɔ mɛ u bɛɛ wɛ̃ mini.
bba	Yenibɑ kpuron biru Yosue Nunin bii, Yinni Gusunɔn sɔm kowo u
bba	ɡu. U kuɑwɑ wɔ̃ɔ wunɔbu kɑ wɔkuru (110).
bba	Ye bɑ turɑ mi, yerɑ bɑ ɡoo wɑ u yɑriɔ wuu ɡen min di.
bba	Mɑ bɑ nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ bɑ nɛɛ, ɑ sun sɔ̃ɔsio mìn di bɑ
bba	rɑ kɑ wuu ɡeni du, kpɑ su nun ɡeɑ kuɑ.
bba	Adɑmɑ kpɑro wi, ù n ɡu, bɑ rɑ mɑɑ kɔ̃sɑ kowɑ n kere
bba	ben bɑɑbɑbɑ. Bũnɑ bɑ rɑ kɑsu bu wiru kpĩiyɑ bu
bba	sɑ̃. Ben ɡɔ̃ru ɡɑ rɑ bɔbiewɑ bu kɑ swɑɑ kɔ̃sɑ ye
bba	Yen biru Ehudu u yɑrɑ dii ten bee tiɑ ɡiɑn di mɑ u ten
bba	Mɑ u duɑ kurɔ win mi, mɑ kurɔ wi, u bekuru suɑ u nùn
bba	sɑɑ yerɑ bɑ bu tɑbu wɔrimɑ.
bba	u bu win sɔmɔ ɡoo ɡɔriɑ wi u bu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ,
bba	ɑmɛniwɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u ɡeruɑ. U nɛɛ, u bɛɛ yɑrɑmɑ
bba	yorun di te i rɑɑ Eɡibitiɡibu diiyɑmmɛ.
bba	Mɑ u Mɑnɑsebɑ kpuro sokusiɑ kɑ Asɛɛbɑ kɑ Sɑbulonibɑ
bba	kɑ Nɛfitɑlibɑ. Mɑ be kpuro bɑ nɑ bɑ mɛnnɑ sɑnnu, bɑ
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ tɔmbu ɡoobɑ wunɔbu ye, yɑ yen kɔbi wurɑmɔ
bba	yerɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u derɑ wɛrɔ be kpuro bɑ ɡoonɑmɔ kɑ
bba	tɑkobi. Mɑ ben ɡɑbu bɑ duki suɑ sere Bɛti Sitɑɔ ye yɑ
bba	wɑ̃ɑ Sererɑn berɑ ɡiɑ Abɛli Mɛholɑn deedeeru Tɑbɑtin
bba	Mɑ Gedeoni u seewɑ u Sebɑki kɑ Sɑlumunɑ ɡo. Yen biru u
bba	burɑ yɑ̃ɑ ni nu wɑ̃ɑ ben yooyoosun wĩinɔ kusiɑ u kɑ
bba	Sɑɑ yerɑ dɑ̃ɑ ni kpuro nu mɑɑ dɑ nu ɑwĩi deemɑ nu
bba	nɛɛ, ɑ nɑ ɑ ko bɛsɛn sunɔ.
bba	Mɑ u win tɔmbu bɔnu kuɑ wuunu itɑ, u derɑ bɑ kukuɑ
bba	yɑkɑsɔ. Ye bɑ Sikɛmuɡii be wɑ bɑ yɑrimɑ wuun di, yerɑ
bba	Mɑ bɑ nɛɛ, sɑ yɛ̃ mɑ sɑ nun torɑriwɑ, ɑ kɑ sun
bba	koowo nɡe mɛ ɑ kĩ. Adɑmɑ ɑ ku de ɑ kun sun fɑɑbɑ kue
bba	Sinɑ boko, n ǹ nɛ nɑ torɑ, wunɑ ɑ torɑ. Domi wunɑ ɑ
bba	ɡbiɑ ɑ sun tɑbu wɔrimɑ. Yen sɔ̃nɑ Yinni Gusunɔ wi u
bba	rɑ tɔmbu sirie u sun siriɑ ɡisɔ bɛsɛ kɑ bɛɛ.
bba	Elonin biru, Abudoni, Hilɛlin bii, Pirɑtoniɡiiwɑ u kuɑ
bba	Win tundo kɑ win mɛro bɑ nùn wisɑ bɑ nɛɛ, tɔn kurɔbu
bba	sɑriwɑ wunɛn mɛro bisibu sɔɔ, ǹ kun mɛ bɛsɛn bweseru
bba	sɔɔ, ɑ kɑ dɑ ɑ kurɔ kɑsu Filisitibɑ sɔɔ be bɑ ku rɑ
bba	Mɑ u doonɑ u sɛ̃usu ɡoobɑ wunɔbu (300) mwɑ u sin sinu
bba	bɔkuɑ yiru yiru. Yerɑ u wii bɔnnu sɔrisi nin sii nin suunu
bba	Mɑ Filisitibɑn sinɑmbu bɑ dɑ kurɔ win mi, bɑ nɛɛ, ɑ
bba	nùn kɔkirio kpɑ ɑ nɔ mìn di win dɑm bɑkɑm mɛ, mu wee,
bba	kɑ nɡe mɛ sɑ ko ko su kɑ nùn nɔmɑ turi. Sɑɑ yerɑ sɑ
bba	ko nùn kɑmiɑ kpɑ bɛsɛn bɑɑwure u nun sii ɡeesun ɡobi
bba	nɔrɔbu kɑ wunɔbu (1.100) wɛ̃.
bba	Yerɑ Sɑnsom u ɑluwɑɑsi wi u win nɔmɑ nɛni sɔ̃ɔwɑ u
bba	nɛɛ, ɑ mɑn yɔ̃suo kpɑ n ɡbere be nɛnɛ bèn wɔllɔ
bba	ɡidɑmbisɑ yeni yɑ sɔ̃ kpɑ n yi ɡbɑlli.
bba	Mɑ tɔnu nɔɔbu be, bɑ doonɑ min di, bɑ dɑ Lɑisiɔ. Bɑ
bba	deemɑ berɑ min tɔmbɑ wɑ̃ɑwɑ bɔri yɛndu sɔɔ,
bba	nɑndɑbu sɑri, nɡe Sidoniɡibu. Domi tɔn tuko ɡoo kun bu
bba	bɑɑsi. Mɛyɑ bɑǹ mɑɑ wɛrɔ ɡoo mɔ turuku. Sidoniɡibu
bba	bɑ kɑ bu tomɑ. Bɑǹ mɑɑ wɑ̃ɑsinɛ kɑ bweseru ɡɑru.
bba	Mɑ bɑ sinɑ bɑ di be yiru ye. Yerɑ dokiri wi, u mɑɑ bu
bba	ɡɔ̃rɑ u nɛɛ, bu kpunɔ sere sisiru bu mɑɑ nuku dobu ko.
bba	Mɑ Isireli be, bɑ bikiɑ bɑ nɛɛ, ɑmɔnɑ dɑɑ kɔ̃sɑ
bba	yenin bweseru yɑ kɑ koorɑ.
bba	Mɑ Bɛnyɑmɛɛ be, bɑ nɛɛ, wee, sɑ mɑɑ bu kɑmiɑ nɡe
bba	yellu. Adɑmɑ Isirelibɑ bɑ nɛɛ, i de su duki su kpɑ bu ben
bba	Yen biruwɑ Isirelibɑ bɑ Bɛnyɑmɛɛ be bɑ dɑ bɑ kukuɑ
bba	Rimɔɔn kpee wɔruɔ ɡɔriɑ bɑ nɛɛ, bu yɑrimɑ, tɑbu
bba	Ye Nɑomi u wɑ mɑ Rutu u yɔ̃rɑwɑ u kɑ nùn dɑ, yerɑ u
bba	Yerɑ Rutu u rɑ n kɑ Boɑsin sɔm kowo tɔn kurɔ be sɔmburu
bba	mɔ̀ sere bɑ kɑ ben ɔɔsu kɑ ɑlikɑmɑ ɡɑ̃ bɑ kpɑ.
bba	Adɑmɑ Nɑomin miyɑ u wɑ̃ɑ u kɑ sɔmbu te dɑɑmɔ.
bba	Mɑ durɔ wi, u nɛɛ, ǹ n mɛn nɑ, nɑ ǹ mɑɑ mu
bba	yɑkiɑmɔ. Domi ye nɑ mɔ nɛn tii yɑ koo rɑ kɑm ko. Yen
bba	sɔ̃, nɑ nun mu deriɑ. A yɑkio ɑ tubi di.
bba	A ku nɛ wunɛn bii ɡɑrisi nɡe bii kɑm. Nɛn nuku sɑnkirɑ
bba	bɑkɑnun sɑɑbuwɑ nɑ kɑnɑru mɔ̀ sere kɑ tɛ̃.
bba	Goo ù n tiɑrɑ wunɛn bweserɔ u koo dɑ u yɛ̃ro wiru
bba	kpĩiyɑwɑ ɡobi fiikon sɔ̃, ǹ kun mɛ dĩɑnun sɔ̃, kpɑ
bba	u ɡere u nɛɛ, ɑ suuru koowo, ɑ de n ko yɑ̃ku kowo ɡoon
bba	sɔm kowo kpɑ nɑ n dɑ dĩɑnu fiiko wɑ n di.
bba	Mɑ Sɑmuɛli u kpɛ̃ɑmɔ. Yinni Gusunɔ u wɑ̃ɑ kɑ wi. U
bba	ǹ mɑɑ dere Sɑmuɛlin ɡɑri yi kɑm wɔri, bɑɑ yin tiɑ.
bba	Yen sɔ̃nɑ Dɑɡonin yɑ̃ku kowobu kɑ be bɑ rɑ du win
bba	dirɔ bu kɑ nùn sɑ̃ kpuro Asidɔduɔ, bɑ ku rɑ mɑɑ dii
bba	kɔnnɔ ɡen deedeeru tɑɑre sere kɑ ɡisɔn ɡisɔ.
bba	Mɑ Bɛti Semɛsiɡibu bɑ nɛɛ, wɑrɑ u koo yɔ̃rɑ Yinni
bba	Gusunɔn wuswɑɑɔ, domi u dɛɛre. Nɡe weren miyɑ kpɑkoro
bba	te, tɑ koo dɑ tɑ̀ n yɑrɑ bɛsɛn min di.
bba	U koo ɡɑbu ɡɔsi bɑ n sɑ̃ɑ tɑbu kowo wuunun wiruɡibu,
bba	kpɑ u ɡɑbu wunɑ bɑ n win ɡbee sɔmɑ mɔ̀ kpɑ ɡɑbu bɑ
bba	n tɑbu yɑ̃nu kɑ tɑbu kɛkɛbɑn yɑ̃nu sekumɔ.
bba	Kɛtɛku ni nu kɔ̃ɔrɑ yen sɔ̃ɔ itɑ ɡisɔ, ɑ ku mɑɑ
bba	nin ɡɑri ko, domi sibɑ nu wɑ. Adɑmɑ ɑ n yɛ̃ mɑ
bba	Isirelibɑn siɑ yɑ ko n wɑ̃ɑ wunɛ kɑ wunɛn bɑɑn
bba	Mɑ u bu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɑmɛniwɑ Gusunɔ bɛɛ
bba	Isirelibɑn Yinni u ɡeruɑ. U nɛɛ, u bɛɛ yɑrɑmɑ
bba	Eɡibitin di mɑ u bɛɛ wɔrɑ Eɡibitiɡibun nɔmɑn di, kɑ
bba	bwesenu kpuro ni nu rɑɑ bɛɛ dɑm dɔremɔn nɔmɑn di.
bba	Tɛ̃ wiyɑ u koo bɛɛ kpɑrɑ, domi nɑ tɔkɔ kuɑ, nɛn seri
bba	bururɑ, nɛn bibɑ mɑɑ bukurɑ nɡe bɛɛ. Wee nɑ bɛɛ
bba	kpɑrɑ sɑɑ nɛn ɑluwɑɑsirun di sere n kɑ ɡirɑri ɡisɔ.
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ Isirelibɑ bɑ wɑ mɑ bɑ ǹ kurɔ, domi
bba	Filisitibɑ bɑ bu sɛ̃ke, mɑ bɑ dɑ bɑ kukuɑ kpee
bba	wɔrusɔ, kɑ ɑwĩi sɔɔ, kɑ kpee bɑɑbɑ sɔɔ, kɑ
bba	wɔrusɔ, sere kɑ dɔkɔ kpirinɔ.
bba	Mɑ be yiru ye, bɑ derɑ Filisitibɑ bɑ bu wɑ. Mɑ Filisiti
bba	be, bɑ nɛɛ, Heberubɑ wee, bɑ yɑrimɑmɔ wɔrusun di mi bɑ
bba	Yen biru u win tɔmbu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, su dɑ su Filisitibɑ
bba	nɑɑ ɡirɑ wɔ̃kuru su bu wɔri sɑ n ben yɑ̃nu ɡurɑmɔ
bba	sere yɑm mu kɑ sɑ̃rɑ. Su ku rɑ ben ɡoo deri, bɑɑ turo.
bba	Mɑ Sɔɔlu u Kenibɑ sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, bu de bu tii wunɑ
bba	Amɑlɛkibɑn min di, kpɑ wi, u ku rɑɑ bu mɛnnɑ u ɡo kpuro
bba	sɑnnu. Domi be, bɑ Isirelibɑ durom kuɑwɑ sɑɑ ye bɑ wee
bba	Eɡibitin di. Mɑ Keni be, bɑ yɑrɑ sɑɑ Amɑlɛkibɑn min di.
bba	nɡe mɛ wunɛn tɑkobi yɑ tɔn kurɔbu ɡɑbun bibu ɡo,
bba	Ye u turɑ mi, u kuɑ win bɔ̃ɔ. Sɔɔlu u nùn kĩɑ ɡem
bba	ɡem mɑ u nùn kuɑ win tɑbu yɑ̃ɑ sɔwo.
bba	Ye Eliɑbu Dɑfidin mɔɔ tɔnwero u nuɑ Dɑfidi u ɡɑri mɔ̀
bba	kɑ tɔn be, u kɑ nùn mɔru kuɑ u nùn bikiɑ u nɛɛ, wɑrɑ
bba	ɑ sere yɑ̃ɑ ɡɔ̃ɔ piibu ɡe deriɑ ɡbɑburɔ. Nɑ wunɛn
bba	ɑnɑyisiru yɛ̃ kɑ wunɛn woo bɔbunu. Nɑ yɛ̃ mɑ ɑ nɑ
bba	Abinɛɛ u wisɑ u nɛɛ, sere kɑ wunɛn wɑ̃ɑru, nɑ ǹ
bba	Mɑ Sɔɔlun ɡɔro be, bɑ wurɑ bɑ nùn Dɑfidin ɡɑri yi
bba	Ye Sɔɔlu nuɑ mɛ, yerɑ win tii u den swɑɑ wɔri u dɔɔ
bba	Rɑmɑɔ. Ye u turɑ dɔkɔ bɑkɑ ye yɑ wɑ̃ɑ Sekuɔ, yerɑ
bba	u bikiɑ u nɛɛ, mɑnɑ Sɑmuɛli kɑ Dɑfidi bɑ wɑ̃ɑ.
bba	Mɑ u sinɑ win ɑyerɔ ɡɑnɑn bɔkuɔ, Abinɛɛ mɑɑ wɑ̃ɑ
bba	win bɔkuɔ, mɑ Yonɑtɑm u sinɑ ben wuswɑɑɔ, ɑdɑmɑ
bba	Dɑfidin sin yerɔ ɡoo sɑri.
bba	Mɑ Dɑfidi nɛɛ, ɑ mɑn ye wɛ̃ɛmɑ domi ɡɑɑ rɑɑ ru
bba	Mɑ u susi u bu ɡo. Yen dɔmɑ te, yɑ̃ku kowobu wɛnɛ kɑ
bba	nɔɔbuwɑ u ɡo be bɑ ben sɑ̃ɑ yɑ̃nu doke.
bba	Mɑ Sɔɔlu u bu wisɑ u nɛɛ, Gusunɔ u bɛɛ domɑru kuɑ
bba	domi nɑ wɑ i nɛn wɔnwɔndu mɔ.
bba	Domi tɔnu u ku rɑ win yibɛrɛ nɔmɑ turi kpɑ u nun yɔ̃su
bba	u doonɑ kɑ ɑlɑfiɑ. Yen sɔ̃nɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u koo nun
bba	ɡeɑ dibu kɔsiɑ ye ɑ mɑn kuɑ minin sɔ̃.
bba	Sere kɑ Yinni Gusunɔn wɑ̃ɑru kɑ mɑɑ wunɛn wɑ̃ɑru,
bba	Yinni Gusunɔwɑ u nun yinɑri ɑ wunɛn yibɛrɛbɑn yɛm
bba	yɑri. Yen sɔ̃ tɛ̃, be bɑ nun tusɑ bɑ wunɛn kɔ̃sɑ
bba	kɑsu, u de bu kɑm ko nɡe Nɑbɑli.
bba	Dɑfidi u mɑɑ nɛɛ, sere kɑ Yinni Gusunɔn wɑ̃ɑru nɑ
bba	yɛ̃ mɑ win tii u koo nùn ɡo tɑbu ɡberɔ, ǹ kun mɛ win
bba	Mɑ Akisi u nùn nɑɑnɛ kuɑ u nɛɛ, Isirelibɑrɑ Dɑfidi u
bba	mɔru seeyɑmɔ. Yen sɔ̃, u ko n sɑ̃ɑwɑ nɛɡii sere kɑ
bba	Adɑmɑ Sɔɔlu u yinɑ u nɛɛ, nɑ ǹ dimɔ. Yerɑ win
bba	bwɑ̃ɑbu kɑ kurɔ wi, bɑ nùn suuru kɑnɑ. Mɑ u ben ɡere
bba	wurɑ u seewɑ tem di u sinɑ kpin yerɔ.
bba	Yerɑ u Dɑfidi wisɑ u nɛɛ, nɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ Eɡibitiɡii, nɑ
bba	kɑ sere sɑ̃ɑ Amɑlɛki ɡoon yoo. Yen sɔ̃ɔ itɑwɑ mini
bba	ye nɛn yinni u kɑ mɑn deri yèn sɔ̃ nɑ bɑrɔ.
bba	Ye Isireli be bɑ wɑ̃ɑ wɔwɑn ɡuruɔ kɑ be bɑ wɑ̃ɑ
bba	Yuudɛnin dɑɑrun ɡuruɔ bɑ nuɑ mɑ ben tɑbu kowobɑ duki
bba	suɑ, Sɔɔlu kɑ win bii tɔn durɔbu bɑ mɑɑ ɡu, yerɑ bɑ
bba	ben wusu deri bɑ duki suɑ. Mɑ Filisitibɑ bɑ nɑ bɑ sinɑ
bba	I ku de bu lɑbɑɑri ye nɔ Gɑtiɔ.
bba	Dɑmɡibɑ wɔrukɑ tɑbu ɡberɔ.
bba	Abinɛɛ u kpɑm nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɑ dɛsiro nɛn bɔkun
bba	di. Domi nɑ̀ n nun so nɑ ɡo, ɑmɔnɑ nɛ kɑ wunɛn mɔɔ
bba	Yen biruwɑ Abinɛɛ u mɑɑ Dɑfidi sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, yinni
bba	sinɑ boko, kon se n dɑ n Isirelibɑ kpuro mɛnnɑ kpɑ bu kɑ
bba	nun ɑrukɑwɑni bɔke bɑ n kɑ wunɛn ɡɑri sɔmburu mɔ̀.
bba	Kpɑ ɑ n bɑndu dii be sɔɔ, ɑ n mɔ̀ ye ɑ kĩ.
bba	Yerɑ tɔn be, bɑ kɑ Isi Bosɛtin wii te dɑ Dɑfidin mi,
bba	Heboroniɔ, bɑ nɛɛ, wunɛn yibɛrɛ Sɔɔlu wi u kɑsu u nun
bba	hunde wunɑ, win bii Isi Bosɛtin wiru wee. Yinni Gusunɔwɑ u
bba	Sɔɔlu kɑ win bweseru mɔru kɔsie ɡisɔ wunɛn sɔ̃.
bba	Dɑfidi u kpɑm Isirelibɑn tɑbu durɔbu kpuro sokɑ u mɛnnɑ
bba	bɑ kuɑ tɔmbu nɔrɔbun subɑ tɛnɑ (30.000).
bba	Yen sɔ̃, ɑ doo ɑ Dɑfidi nɛn sɔm kowo sɔ̃ ɑ nɛɛ, nɛ
bba	Gusunɔ wɔllu kɑ tem Yinni, nɛnɑ nɑ yeni ɡerumɔ. Yɑ̃ɑ
bba	kpɑrɑbun diyɑ nɑ nùn wunɑmɑ u n kɑ sɑ̃ɑ nɛn tɔmbu
bba	Ye Toi, Hɑmɑtin sinɑ boko u nuɑ mɑ Dɑfidi u Hɑdɑdesɛɛn
bba	yerɑ Hɑnunin sinɑ ɑsɑkpɔbu bɑ nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ bɑ nɛɛ,
bba	ɑ tɑmɑɑ Dɑfidin bwɑ̃ɑ be, bɑ nɑwɑ bu kɑ wunɛn tundo
bba	bɛɛrɛ wɛ̃? A ǹ yɛ̃ bɑ nɑwɑ bu kɑ bɛsɛn wuun
bba	sɑriɑ ɡiɑ, kpɑ bu ɡu wɔrimɑ bu mwɑ?
bba	Mɑ Dɑfidi u nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ǹ n mɛn nɑ, ɑ kpɑm
bba	kpunɔ mini ɡisɔ kpɑ ɑ doonɑ siɑ. Mɑ Uri u sinɑ
bba	Adɑmɑ ye ɑ kuɑ mi, yɑ derɑ Yinni Gusunɔn yibɛrɛbɑ bɑ
bba	win yĩsiru ɡɑri kɑm ɡerusi. Yen sɔ̃, u koo de bii wi
bba	kurɔ wi, u kɑ nun mɑrɑ mi, u ɡbi.
bba	Sɑɑ yerɑ Amɔɔ u Tɑmɑɑ sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɑ kɑ kirɑ
bba	ni nɑ dii sɔɔwɔ kpɑ n nu mwɑ wunɛn nɔmun di, n sere di.
bba	Yen sɔ̃ tɛ̃, ɑ ku ɡɔ̃ru doke mɑ wunɛn bibu kpurowɑ
bba	bɑ ɡu. Adɑmɑ ɑ n yɛ̃ mɑ Amɔɔ tɔnɑwɑ u ɡu.
bba	Yerɑ sinɑ boko u nɛɛ, n ǹ Yoɑbuwɑ u nun yenibɑ
bba	Mɑ u tɔmbu ɡoobu (200) kɑnɑ Yerusɑlɛmun di, bɑ kɑ nùn
bba	dɑ Heboroni mi. Adɑmɑ bɑ ǹ yɛ̃ ye u niɑ sɑ̃ɑ win
bba	Mɑ Sibɑ u nùn wisɑ u nɛɛ, yinni, kɛtɛku nini, nu
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ ni wunɛn yɛnuɡibu bɑ koo sɔni. Pɛ̃ɛ yeni kɑ
bba	dɑ̃ɑ bii nini, yɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ ye wunɛn tɑbu kowobu bɑ koo
bba	di. Be bɑ mɑɑ wɑsirɑ ɡbɑburɔ, tɑm mɛniwɑ bɑ koo nɔ,
bba	Wunɛn tii, ɑ wunɛn tundo kɑ win tɔmbu yɛ̃ mɑ bɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ tɑbu durɔbu. Bɑ kɔ̃ruɑwɑ nɡe ɡbeeku yɑɑ
bba	ɡɔbɑ ye bɑ binu mwɑɑri. Yen biru ɑ yɛ̃ mɑ wunɛn tundo
bba	wi, u sɑ̃ɑwɑ tɑbun sɑriɑ yɛ̃ro. U ǹ wurɑmɔ u kpunɑ
bba	Sinɑ boko u Yoɑbu kɑ Abisɑi kɑ Itɑi woodɑ yeni wɛ̃ u
bba	nɛɛ, i ku kɑ Abusɑlɔmu bii ɑluwɑɑsi wi bɔɔbɔm ko, ì
bba	Sinɑ boko u nùn wisɑ u nɛɛ, lɑbɑɑri dorɑ win tii u
bba	Bɛnyɑmɛɛn bweseru sɔɔ be bɑ Simɛi swĩimɑ bɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ tɔmbu nɔrɔbu (1.000) kɑ sere Sibɑ wi u rɑɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑ Sɔɔlun sɔm kowo wi kɑ mɑɑ win bibu wɔkurɑ
bba	nɔɔbu kɑ win sɔm kowobu yɛndu. Tɔn be kpurowɑ bɑ ɡbiɑ
bba	bɑ sinɑ boko turiɑ Yuudɛnin dɑɑru mi.
bba	Sɑɑ ye sɔɔ, tɔn kɔ̃so ɡoo wɑ̃ɑ Bɛnyɑmɛɛn bweseru
bba	sɔɔ, win yĩsirɑ Sebɑ, Bikirin bii. Yerɑ u kɔbɑ so u
bba	Mɑ kurɔ wi, u dɑ u tɔmbu mɛnnɑ kɑ bwisi bɑ dɑ Sebɑn
bba	mi, bɑ win wiru burɑ bɑ tu Yoɑbu kɑsɑ kuɑmɑ. Yerɑ
bba	Yoɑbu u kɔbɑ so mɑ win tɑbu kowobu bɑ yɑrinɑ bɑ wuu ɡe
bba	deri. Ben bɑɑwure u wurɑ win yɛnuɔ. Mɑ Yoɑbun tii u
bba	ɡɔsirɑ Yerusɑlɛmuɔ u dɑ sinɑ bokon mi.
bba	Womu ɡeniwɑ Dɑfidi u Yinni Gusunɔ kuɑ sɑnɑm mɛ u nùn
bba	wɔrɑ sɑɑ win yibɛrɛbɑn nɔmɑn di, n mɑm nɛɛre Sɔɔlu.
bba	Mɑ u sɑrɑmɑ u ɡuru wii bɑkɑru tɑɑkumɔ.
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ, wunɑ ɑ rɑ mɑn fɑɑbɑ ko nɡe tɛrɛru.
bba	ben kuku yerun di bɑ n diirumɔ.
bba	Ye nɑ kĩ kpuro u rɑ mɑn kuewɑ.
bba	kɑ Sɑɑmɔɔ, Akoɑsiɡii, kɑ Mɑhɑrɑi, Nɛtofɑɡii,
bba	Yen dɔmɑ terɑ Gɑdi u dɑ Dɑfidin mi, u nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ u
bba	nɛɛ, ɑ Yinni Gusunɔ yɑ̃ku yeru kuo Arɑfunɑ Yebusin doo
bba	Mɑ bɑ sinɑ boko sɔ̃ɔwɑ bɑ nɛɛ, Gusunɔn sɔmɔ
bba	Nɑtɑni wee, u tunumɑ. Yerɑ u sinɑ boko yiirɑ u wuswɑɑ
bba	Mɑ Sɑlomɔɔ u nɛɛ, ù n tii nɛnuɑ dee dee, bɑɑ win
bba	wirun seri tiɑ yɑ ǹ wɔrumɑmɔ. Adɑmɑ sɑ̀ n kɔ̃sɑ
bba	ɡɑɑ wɑ win min di, u koo ɡbiwɑ.
bba	Mɑ Sɑlomɔɔ wi, u Bɛnɑyɑ Yehoyɑdɑn bii ɡɔrɑ u dɑ u
bba	Adoniyɑ ɡo. Mɑ u dɑ u nùn ɡo.
bba	Sɔ̃ɔ teeru Sɑlomɔɔ sinɑ boko u seewɑ u dɑ Gɑbɑoniɔ u
bba	kɑ yɑ̃kuru ko. Domi miyɑ yɑ̃ku yee bɑkɑrɑ wɑ̃ɑ.
bba	Yɑ̃ku dɔ̃ɔ mwɑɑrɑruɡinu dɑbi dɑbinɑ u dɔmɑ te kuɑ
bba	Elihorɛfu kɑ Akiyɑ, Sisɑn bibu bɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ tire yorobu.
bba	Gusunɔ u Sɑlomɔɔ bwisi kɑ lɑɑkɑri kɑ yɛ̃ɛ bɑkɑru
bba	Ye bɑ dii te bɑnimɔ, bɑ tu bɑnɑwɑ kɑ kpee ni bɑ rɑɑ
bba	dɑ̃kɑ ten sɔ̃. Yen sɔ̃nɑ bɑ ǹ sɔm yɑ̃nu ɡɑnun
bba	dɑmu nuɑ mi, ni bɑ kuɑ kɑ sisu, bɑɑ mɑtɑlɑkɑ ǹ kun
bba	Mɑ bɑ dii te bɑnɑ bɑ kpɑ kɑ ten bɑɑyere kpuro nɡe mɛ
bba	bɑ ten kpunɑɑ yi, win bɑndun wɔ̃ɔ wɔkurɑ tiɑsen suru
bba	Bɑ yɔ̃rɑtiɑ yen bɑɑyeren wɔllɔ nɔɔ ɡɑɡu seeyɑ
bba	bwɛrɛrɛ. Gen dukum mu sɑ̃ɑwɑ ɡɔm soo teeru, mɑ ɡen
bba	yɑsum mu sɑ̃ɑ ɡɔm soo teeru kɑ bɔnu. Miyɑ bɑ koo boo
bba	ɡe sɔndi. Sii fɛfɛrɛfɛ si bɑ wɑsi yɔ̃rɑtii yin
bba	kɑdiri sɔɔ mi, ɡoonu nnɛwɑ su mɔ. Nin dɛ̃ɛbu kɑ
bba	yɑsum n nɛwɑ. Sin wɔllɔwɑ bɑ burɑru koosi.
bba	kɑ dii te tɑ dɛɛre ɡem ɡem ɡɑmbobɑn sɔretii. Kɑ sere
bba	mɑɑ ɡɑmbo ni nu tien sɔretii.
bba	Ǹ n mɛn nɑ, Gusunɔ bɛsɛn Yinni, ɑ de wunɛn ɡɑri yi ɑ
bba	nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ mi kpuro, yi koorɑ.
bba	U bɛsɛn bwɛ̃rɑ ɡɔsio win mi ɡiɑ kpɑ su kpĩ su win
bba	swɛɛ kpuro swĩi su win woodɑbɑ kɑ win yiirebu kpuro mɛm
bba	nɔɔwɑ bi u bɛsɛn bɑɑbɑbɑ wɛ̃.
bba	Be u ɡɔsɑ bu kɑ yoo sɔmɑ ye kpɑrɑ, bɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ
bba	nɛɛrɑ wunɔbu kɑ weerɑɑkuru (550).
bba	Mɑ Sɑlomɔɔ u tɑbu kɛkɛbɑ kɑsu yi dumi ɡɑwe kɑ mɑɑ
bba	mɑɑsɔbu. Tɑbu kɛkɛ yen ɡeerɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ nɔrɔbu kɑ
bba	nɛɛru (1.400). Mɑɑsɔ be, bɑ mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ nɔrɔbun subɑ
bba	wɔkurɑ yiru (12.000). Mɑ u mɑɑsɔ be yi yi wuu mɑrosɔ mi
bba	win tɑbu kɛkɛ yi wɑ̃ɑ kɑ sere mɑɑ Yerusɑlɛmuɔ mi win
bba	Ye u Yeroboɑmu wɑ u sɑ̃ɑ ɑluwɑɑsi dɑmɡii u mɑɑ
bba	sɔmburu mɔ̀ mi kɑ hɑniɑ, yerɑ u nùn kuɑ Mɑnɑse kɑ
bba	Efɑrɑimun bwese kɛrɑn wiruɡii bu kɑ sɔmbu te ko.
bba	Adɑmɑ win sɑɑrɑsi ben bwisiyɑ u kɑ sɔmburu kuɑ mɑ u
bba	nɛɛ, nɛn tundo u rɑɑ bɛɛ yoo sɔmɑ koosiɑ. Adɑmɑ
bba	tɛ̃, nɛɡirɑ tɑ koo kerɑ. U rɑɑ bɛɛ sɛɛyɑsiɑ kɑ
bba	yii sɛnnu. Adɑmɑ nɛ, som kpɑkiyɑ kon kɑ bɛɛ
bba	Yerɑ yɑ̃ku yee te, tɑ bɛsirɑ, mɑ ten yɑ̃ku torom mɛ mu
bba	wɑ̃ɑ wɔllɔ mu pusi yɑm kpuro nɡe mɛ Yinni Gusunɔ u
bba	rɑɑ ɡeruɑ sɑɑ sɔmɔ win nɔɔn di.
bba	Mɑ durɔ wi, u ɡoo te suɑ u sɔndi win kɛtɛku wɔllɔ u kɑ
bba	tu nɑ win wuuɔ, u sikɑ siki wɔru ɡe u rɑɑ ɡbɑ win tiin
bba	Roboɑmun bɑndun wɔ̃ɔ nɔɔbuse sɔɔrɑ Sisɑki Eɡibitin
bba	sinɑ boko u nɑ u Yerusɑlɛmu tɑbu wɔri.
bba	mɑ u kpunɑ u ɡu. Bɑ nùn sikuɑ win bɑɑbɑbɑn sikɑɔ win
bba	sikɑdo Dɑfidin wuuɔ. Mɑ win bii Yosɑfɑti u ɡɔnɑ sinɑ.

bba	sɑ̃ɑwɔ. Ǹ n mɑɑ Bɑɑlin nɑ, i nùn sɑ̃ɑwɔ.

bba	bii be bɑ burɑm bo, bɑ kuɑ wi Bɛni Hɑdɑdiɡibu.

bba	sɔ̃ Siriɡibu bɑ nɛɛ, u sɑ̃ɑwɑ ɡuunun yinni, yen
bba	sɔ̃nɑ u koo be tɑbu kowo dɑbi te bɛɛ nɔmu bɛriɑ kpɑ i
bba	ɡiɑ mɑ wiyɑ u sɑ̃ɑ kpuron Yinni.
bba	U nun wisɑ u nɛɛ, Nɑbɔtiwɑ nɑ sɔ̃ɔwɑ nɑ nɛɛ, u
bba	mɑn win resɛm ɡbɑɑru derio. Kpɑ n nùn ten ɡobi kɔsiɑ,

bba	mini, bɛɛn bɑɑwure u ɡɑri yi swɑɑ suo.

bba	ben wɑ̃ɑru sɔɔ, mɑ bɑ nun mɛm nɔɔwɑmmɛ nɡe mɛ wi,
bba	bɑ n nuku dobu mɔ̀ doo nɔɔru sɔ.
bba	U tem mi ɡɑ̃ɑnu ku rɑ kpin wuu ɡe bɑ mɔ̀ Tɑdimɔri
bba	bɑnɑ kɑ sere mɑɑ Hɑmɑtin wuu sìn mi bɑ ko n dɑ win
bba	Yerɑ u mɑɑ sinɑ kitɑru kuɑ kɑ suunu donnu, mɑ u tu wurɑ
bba	Nɡe mɛyɑ Roboɑmu u yinɑ u tɔn beɡii swɑɑ dɑki, domi
bba	Yinni Gusunɔwɑ u derɑ n koorɑ mɛ, kpɑ win ɡɑri yi kɑ
bba	koorɑ yi u rɑɑ Yeroboɑmu, Nɛbɑtin bii sɔ̃ɔwɑ sɑɑ
bba	Roboɑmu u Mɑhɑlɑti suɑ kurɔ. Mɑhɑlɑtin tundon yĩsirɑ
bba	Yerimɔti, Dɑfidin bii. Win mɛron yĩsirɑ Abihɑili, Eliɑbun
bba	Tɛ̃, i tɑmɑɑ i ko i kɑ bɑn te yinɑ te Yinni Gusunɔ u
bba	Dɑfidin bibun bweseru nɔɔ mwɛɛru kuɑ. Geemɑ i dɑbi too.
bba	Mɑ i kɛtɛn bwɑ̃ɑrokunu mɔ ni Yeroboɑmu u bɛɛ kuɑ kɑ
bba	wurɑ nu n sɑ̃ɑ bɛɛn yinnibu.
bba	Asɑ kɑ win tɔmbu bɑ wuu si su wɑ̃ɑ Gerɑɔ wɔri bɑ
bba	kɔsukɑ. Mɑ bɑ dukiɑ bɑkɑ ɡurɑ. Domi sin tɔmbɑ Yinni
bba	Gusunɔn bɛrum kuɑ bɑ nɑndɑ.
bba	Mɑ Asɑ u kɑ Gusunɔn sɔmɔ wi mɔru kuɑ ɡem ɡem. Mɑ u
bba	derɑ bɑ nùn pirisɔm doke. Sɑɑ ye sɔɔrɑ u mɑɑ
bba	Mɑ bɑ wisɑ bɑ nɛɛ, ɑ doo, Gusunɔ u koo nun ɡe nɔmu
bba	Yenibɑn biru, Isirelibɑn sinɑ boko kɑ Yosɑfɑti, Yudɑbɑn
bba	sinɑ boko bɑ seewɑ bɑ tɑɑ bi dɑ Rɑmɔtiɔ Gɑlɑdin
bba	Yerɑ Yinni Gusunɔn Hunde u Yɑɑsiɛli, Sɑkɑrin bii yɔɔwɑ
bba	tɔmbun suunu sɔɔ. Yɑɑsiɛli wi, u sɑ̃ɑwɑ Asɑfun
bba	bweseru, Lefibɑ sɔɔ. Win sikɑdobɑrɑ Bɛnɑyɑ kɑ Yeyɛli
bba	Isirelibɑn sinɑmbun yirɑ u swĩi nɡe mɛ Akɑbun yɛnuɡibu
bba	bɑ kuɑ. Domi Akɑbun bii tɔn kurɔwɑ u suɑ kurɔ. Kɔ̃sɑ
bba	u kuɑ Yinni Gusunɔn wuswɑɑɔ.
bba	Bɑ Yudɑn tem bukiɑnɑ. Mɑ bɑ Lefibɑ mɛnnɑ sɑɑ Yudɑn
bba	wusu kpuron di kɑ sere Isirelibɑn yɛnu yɛ̃robu. Be kpuro
bba	Mɑ bɑ kpɑrɑ Yudɑɔ kɑ Yerusɑlɛmuɔ bɑ nɛɛ, bu kɑ
bba	ɡobi yi nɑ yi Mɔwisi Gusunɔn sɔm kowo u Isirelibɑ bure
bba	ɡbɑburɔ mi ɡɑ̃ɑnu ku rɑ kpi.
bba	Mɑ Amɑsiɑ u wɔruɡɔru seewɑ u win tɔmbu kpɑrɑ mɑ u dɑ
bba	u wɑ̃ɑ wɔwɑɔ ye bɑ mɔ̀ Bɔru. Miyɑ u tɔmbu nɔrɔbun
bba	subɑ wɔkuru (10.000) ɡo Seirin bibun bweseru sɔɔ.
bba	Yɛnu yɛ̃robu kɑ tɑbu durɔ wɔruɡɔbɑ, be kpuron ɡeerɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ nɔrɔbun subɑ yiru kɑ nɑtɑ (2.600).
bba	Yerɑ i kĩ tɛ̃, Yudɑ be, kɑ Yerusɑlɛmuɡii be, bu ko
bba	bɛɛn yobu? I ǹ tɑmɑɑ i Gusunɔ bɛɛn Yinni torɑri?
bba	kɑ Simuri kɑ Yeyɛli Elisɑfɑnin bibun bweseru sɔɔ kɑ
bba	Sɑkɑri kɑ Mɑtɑniɑ Asɑfun bibun bweseru sɔɔ
bba	Mɑ bɑ derɑ bɑ kpɑrɑ Isirelin tem kpuro sɔɔ sɑɑ Beri
bba	Sebɑn di n kɑ dɑ sere Dɑnuɔ, tɔmbu bu kɑ nɑ
bba	Yerusɑlɛmuɔ bu Gusunɔ Isirelibɑn Yinni Gɔɔ sɑrɑribun
bba	tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑ te diiyɑ. Domi tɔn dɑbiru tɑ ku rɑ rɑɑ
bba	mɑɑ tu di nɡe mɛ bɑ yoruɑ bu ko.
bba	Mɑ Esekiɑsi u yɑ̃ku kowobu kɑ Lefi be bikiɑ u nɛɛ, subu
bba	Sɑnkeribu u tireru yoruɑ u kɑ Gusunɔ Isirelibɑn Yinni
bba	wɔmɛ. U nɛɛ, nɡe mɛ bwese ni nu tien bũnu nu ǹ kpĩɑ
bba	nu nin tɔmbu wɔre win nɔmɑn di, nɡe mɛyɑ Gusunɔ,
bba	Esekiɑsin Yinni u ǹ mɑɑ kpɛ̃ u bu wɔrɑ win nɔmɑn di.
bba	Mɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u ɡɔ̃ru ɡɔsiɑ u win kɑnɑru mwɑ, u kɑ
bba	nùn wurɑ Yerusɑlɛmuɔ win bɑndu sɔɔ. Sɑɑ ye sɔɔrɑ
bba	Mɑnɑse u ɡiɑ mɑ Gusunɔwɑ u sɑ̃ɑ Yinni.
bba	Yen biru, yɑ̃ku kowo Hilikiyɑ u mɑɑ mɑn tireru ɡɑru
bba	Yen biruwɑ bɑ ben tiiɡiɑ kɑ yɑ̃ku kowobuɡiɑ yikuɑ.
bba	Domi yɑ̃ku kowo Aronin bibu bɑ sɔmburu kuɑ sere kɑ
bba	wɔ̃kurɔ. Bɑ yɑ̃ku dɔ̃ɔ mwɑɑrɑruɡinu kɑ yɑɑ ɡum
bba	yɑ̃kunu mɔ̀. Yen sɔ̃nɑ Lefibɑ bɑ bu yɑɑ yikuɑmmɛ.
bba	Nɛbukɑnɛsɑɑ u Yinni Gusunɔn sɑ̃ɑ yerun ɑrumɑni ɡurɑ
bba	bɑkɑ kɑ piibu kɑ ben sinɑ kpɑɑrun ɑrumɑni kɑ sinɑ
bba	bokon tiiɡiɑ kɑ sere mɑɑ win sinɑ bwɑ̃ɑbuɡiɑ.
bba	Biɡifɑin bweseru sɔɔ, bɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ tɔmbu nɔrɔbun subɑ
bba	yiru kɑ weerɑɑkuru kɑ nɔɔbɑ tiɑ (2.056).
bba	kɑ Kɛrɔsi kɑ Siɑɑ kɑ Pɑdoni
bba	Nɡe mɛyɑ sɑɑ suru nɔɔbɑ yirusen tɔ̃ɔ ɡbiikirun di,
bba	bɑ Yinni Gusunɔ yɑ̃ku dɔ̃ɔ mwɑɑrɑruɡinu kuɑmmɛ
bba	bɑɑ mɛ bɑ ǹ ɡinɑ sɑ̃ɑ yee ten kpɛɛkpɛɛku swĩi.
bba	Sɑɑ ye sɔɔ, Gusunɔn sɔmɔ Asee kɑ Sɑkɑri Idon bii bɑ
bba	Gusunɔn ɡɑri ɡeruɑ kɑ Gusunɔ Isirelibɑn Yinnin yĩsiru
bba	Yerusɑlɛmuɔ kɑ Yudɑbɑn tem kpuro sɔɔ.
bba	Gusunɔn sɔmɔbu Asee kɑ Sɑkɑri, Idon bii bɑ Isirelibɑn
bba	wiruɡibu dɑm kɑ̃ bɑ kɑ sɑ̃ɑ yee te bɑnɑ bɑ kpɑ mɑm
bba	mɑm. Bɑ tu bɑnɑwɑ nɡe mɛ Gusunɔ Isirelibɑn Yinni u
bba	ɡeruɑ kɑ nɡe mɛ Pɛɛsin sinɑm beni, Sirusi kɑ Dɑrusi
bba	kɑ Aɑtɑsɛsi bɑ yen woodɑ yi.
bba	Ɛsidɑrɑsi u nɛɛ, i Gusunɔ bɛsɛn bɑɑbɑbɑn Yinni
bba	siɑro. U derɑ sinɑ boko u win sɑ̃ɑ yee te tɑ wɑ̃ɑ
bba	kɑ ɡbɛ̃ɛ bɑsilɑnu yɛndu ni bɑ kuɑ kɑ wurɑ. Yen
bba	ɡeerɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ wurɑn ɡobi nɔrɔbu (1.000) kɑ sere boo
bba	sii ɡɑnduɡisu yiru si su bɑllimɔ. Boo si, su kɑ wurɑɡisu
bba	Yen biru, Ɛsidɑrɑsi u yɑrɑ Gusunɔn sɑ̃ɑ yerun di u dɑ
bba	Yokɑnɑni Eliɑsibun biin dirɔ. Sɑnɑm mɛ u duɑ mi, u ǹ
bba	dĩɑnu di, u ǹ mɑɑ nim nɔrɑ. Domi win nuki sɑnkire
bba	Isireli be bɑ yoru mwɛɛrɑn dɑɑ kɔ̃sɑ ye bɑ kuɑn sɔ̃.
bba	kɑ Bɛnɑyɑ kɑ Bediɑ kɑ Keluhu
bba	Mɑ nɑ nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ sɑɑ ye kon wurɑmɑ. Mɑ u wurɑ n dɑ.
bba	Mɑɑkiyɑ Rekɑbun bii wi u sɑ̃ɑ Bɛti Hɑkerɛmun berɑn
bba	tem yɛ̃ro u kɔnnɔ ɡèn min di bɑ rɑ kubɑnu yɑri
bba	sɔnwɑ. Mɑ u ɡen kɑdiribɑ kuɑ u doke kɑ ɡen kɔkɔrɔbɑ
bba	kɑ sere mɑɑ ɡen sɛ̃retii.
bba	sere bɛsɛn sɔm kowobɑ wɑsirɑ kɑ nin ɡurɑbu.
bba	Mɑ be kpuro bɑ wurɑ bɑ nɛɛ, ɑmi, n yɛ̃ro koowo mɛsum.
bba	Nɑ bu sɔ̃ɔwɑ nɑ nɛɛ, bɑ ǹ Yerusɑlɛmun kɔnnɔsu
bba	kɛniɑmɔ mɑ n kun mɔ sɔ̃ɔ u yɑrɑ. Yokɑ bɑ koo su
bba	kɛnɛwɑ kɔnnɔ kɔ̃sobu bu sere doonɑ. Yen biru, bɑ koo
bba	Yerusɑlɛmuɡibu bikiɑ bu wuu kɔ̃su, ben bɑɑwure u n yɔ̃
bba	Nɛbo yeɔnɔɡibu bɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ tɔmbu weerɑɑkuru kɑ yiru
bba	Yɑ̃ku kowobu sɔɔ, ɡɑbɑ mɑɑ wɑ̃ɑ be bɑ ǹ kpĩɑ
bba	bɑ ben bweserun tɔ̃kɑ wunɑnɛ. Berɑ Hobɑyɑn bibun
bba	bweseru kɑ Hɑkɔtuɡiru kɑ Bɑɑsilɑiɡiru. Bɑ bwese te
bba	sokɑ Bɑɑsilɑi yèn sɔ̃ ben sikɑdo u Bɑɑsilɑi
bba	Gɑlɑdiɡiin bii wɔndiɑ suɑ kurɔ.
bba	Yen biru, bɑ bu Yinni Gusunɔn ɡɑri ɡɑriɑ kɔbɑ itɑn
bba	sɑkɑ bɑ yɔ̃ bɑ swɑɑ dɑki. Mɑ bɑ yiirɑ wi, ben Yinnin
bba	wuswɑɑɔ bɑ suuru kɑnɑ sere kɔbɑ itɑ mɑɑ.
bba	Mɑ ɑ sɔm mɑɑmɑɑkiɡinu kuɑ ɑ kɑ ben sunɔ
bba	Adɑmɑ kɑ mɛ, ɑ ǹ bu deri.
bba	Mɑ ɑ derɑ bɑ duɑ Kɑnɑnin temɔ
bba	Mɑ ɑ ben nɔɔ nuɑ wɔllun di,
bba	kɑ Hodiyɑ kɑ Hɑsumu kɑ Bɛsɑi
bba	Yoɛli Sikirin biiwɑ u sɑ̃ɑ ben kpɑro. Mɑ Yudɑ Senuɑn
bba	bii u mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ ben wiruɡii yiruse.
bba	kɑ Semɑyɑ kɑ Yoyɑribu kɑ Yedɑyɑ
bba	Ye bɑ tunumɑ kɔnnɔwɔ ɡe bɑ mɔ̀ Bwiɑ, yerɑ bɑ dɑ
bba	Dɑfidin wuun yɔɔ yerɔ mɑ bɑ yɔɔwɑ ɡɑnɑ yen wɔllɔ
bba	bɑ kɑ Dɑfidin sinɑ kpɑɑru tuke, mɑ bɑ dɑ kɔnnɔwɔ ɡe
bba	bɑ mɔ̀ Nim, sɔ̃ɔ yɑri yeru ɡiɑ.
bba	Yerɑ kiɑ bwese bwesekɑn dɔrobu bɑ kpunɑ wuun biruɔ nɡe
bba	Domi tɔn kurɔbu kpuro bɑ̀ n nuɑ ye Fɑsiti u kuɑ, bɑ koo
bba	sewɑ bu ben durɔbu ɡɛm. Bɑ ǹ mɑɑ bu mɛm nɔɔwɑmmɛ.
bba	Kpɑ bu kɑ tii yinɑ bu nɛɛ, ye sinɑ boko u rɑɑ win kurɔ
bba	Yenibɑn biru, Asuresi u Hɑmɛdɑtɑn bii wi u sɑ̃ɑ
bba	Aɡɑɡin bweseru wɔlle suɑ. Mɑ u nùn kuɑ yiruse win bɑndu
bba	u doo u Yuubɑ kpuro mɛnnɑ be bɑ wɑ̃ɑ Susi mi, kpɑ bu
bba	nɔɔ bɔke win sɔ̃, sɔ̃ɔ sɔɔ itɑ kɑ wɔ̃kuru itɑ, bu
bba	ku dĩɑnu di, bu ku mɑɑ nim nɔ. Wi kɑ mɑɑ win sɔm kowobu
bba	bɑ koo mɑɑ ko mɛsum. Yen biru, kpɑ u dɑ sinɑ bokon mi,
bba	bɑɑ mɛ woodɑ yɑ mɛ yinɑ. Ù n koo ɡbin nɑ, kpɑ u ɡbi.
bba	Yerɑ sinɑ boko u Hɑmɑni sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, tɛ̃, ɑ seewo
bba	ɑ yɑ̃ɑ ni kɑ dumɑ ye suɑ kpɑ ɑ Yuu wi kuɑ nɡe mɛ ɑ
bba	ɡeruɑ mi. Bɑɑ yen ɡɑ̃ɑ piibu ɑ ku rɑ duɑri. U wɑ̃ɑ
bba	sinɑ kpɑɑ kɔnnɔwɔ u sɔmburu mɔ̀ mi.
bba	Berɑ mi tire te, tɑ ɡesi turɑ, bɑ koo ten ɡɑri
bba	ɡɑrisiwɑ woodɑ kpɑ bu de tɔmbu kpuro bɑ n ye yɛ̃. Kpɑ
bba	Yuubɑ bɑ n sɔɔru sɑ̃ɑ bu kɑ ben yibɛrɛbɑ mɔru
bba	Yen sɔ̃nɑ bɑ tɔ̃ɔ ni sokɑ Purimu ben tɛtɛ dumin sɔ̃.
bba	Sɑɑ yè sɔɔ wini mɑɑ ɡɑri ɡerumɔ u ǹ kpɑ, kpɑo
bba	mɑɑ kɑ tunumɑ. U nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, wunɛn bibɑ sɔ̃
bba	bɑ dimɔ bɑ nɔrumɔ ben tɔnweron dirɔ,
bba	U ku de yɑm bururɑm mu mɑɑ koorɑ te sɔɔ.
bba	bɑ ǹ mɑɑ be bɑ bu dɑm dɔremɔn nɔɔ nɔɔmɔ.
bba	ǹ kun mɛ bɑ ɡemɡibu mwɛɛrɑ bɑ kpeerɑsiɑ.
bba	U ǹ bwisi kpuro wɑ u kɑ ɡu.
bba	Adɑmɑ Gusunɔ u rɑ dɑm sɑriruɡii ɡɑnɛ ben tɑbu
bba	kɑ nɛn wɑhɑlɑ kpuro kilo sɔndi,
bba	Purɑn sɑɑ, kpɑ tɑ n nim yibumɔ bɑɑmɑn di mɛ mu dɛɛre.
bba	Suru dɑbinu nɑ wɑ̃ɑ nɔni swɑ̃ɑru sɔɔ.
bba	Nɛn wɑ̃ɑrɑ kun sɑ̃ɑ ɡɑ̃ɑnu, ɑ mɑn derio sɛ̃ɛ.
bba	kpɑ ɑ lɑɑkɑri ko ɑ wɑ wɑhɑlɑ ye ben sikɑdobɑ bɑ
bba	Domi u mɑn wɔri nɡe woo ɡunɑ.
bba	kɑ mɛ, u koo mɑn surewɑ pɔtɔkɔ sɔɔ,
bba	Yerɑ ɑ kĩ ɑ mɑn kpeerɑsiɑ, n ɡɔsiɑ tuɑ?
bba	Yɑm bururɑm mɛ mu wɑ̃ɑ mi,
bba	Bɑ rɑ n ben tiin dɑm sɑ̃ɑmɔ.
bba	kɑ mɛ, u koo bɛɛ tɑɑrɛ wɛ̃.
bba	Wɑrɑ ɑ nɑɑ swĩi. Yɑkɑ ɡbebusu?
bba	Ù n ɡu, mɑnɑ u rɑ n wɑ̃ɑ.
bba	Mɛyɑ bɑ̀ n mɑɑ wɑ̃ɑ sekuru sɔɔ,
bba	Tɔnu u koo kpĩ u n dɛɛre?
bba	sìn diɑ bɑ deri, mɑ yɑ wɔrumɑm dɔɔ.
bba	Wee tɛ̃, Gusunɔ u derɑ nɑ dɑm dwiiyɑ.
bba	Nɛn kpɑɑsibu bɑ mɑn yɑɑkoru mɔ̀.
bba	Wee himbɑ ye nɑ rɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ ye kpuro yɑ kɑm kuɑ.
bba	kpɑ yen wɛ̃ɛ yi nùn tɛ̃ke.
bba	kpɑ i n mɑn tɔ̃yɑ mɔ̀ kɑ bɛɛn ɡɑri sɑɑrinu.
bba	Nɑ̀ n nɛn sɔm kowo sokɑ, u ku rɑ wure.
bba	Tɔn ben bweseru, bɑ ǹ doo nɔɔru mɔ ro?
bba	Bɑɑ Gusunɔ ù n kɑ nùn mɔru kuɑ,
bba	Dɑm kpuroɡii koo nun wunɛn yellun wɑ̃ɑru wesiɑ.
bba	Nɑ̀ n mɑɑ dɑ sɔ̃ɔ duu yerɔ,
bba	Mɑ bɑ ɡɔminibun nɛɛ tɔrubɑ mwɑɑmɔ.
bba	Yɑm wɔ̃kuru sɔɔrɑ ɡbɛnɔ u rɑ diɑ kɔsuku.
bba	U rɑ de bɔri yɛndu tɑ n wɑ̃ɑ sere wɔllun sɔɔ sɔɔwɔ.
bba	Kɑ win dɑmɑ u rɑ nim wɔ̃kun nim kɔsuku.
bba	Mbɑn sɔ̃nɑ i ɡɑri ɡerumɔ yi yi ǹ ɑsɑnsi mɔ.
bba	kpɑ bu wɔru ɡbe sere tem sɔɔwɔ,
bba	kɑɑ sere ɡere kpee ɡobiɡii ni bɑ sokumɔ korɑi kɑ
bba	Sɑɑ ye sɔɔ, Gusunɔ Dɑm kpuroɡii u kɑ mɑn wɑ̃ɑ,
bba	Kpɑ kɑkoru tɑ n wɑ̃ɑ nɛn kɑ̃ɑsin wɔllɔ.
bba	ǹ kun mɛ nɡe be bɑ ɡɛmɑ bɑ ɡirɑ wuun di.
bba	Wee ɑ derɑ woo ɡunɑ yɑ mɑn suɑ yɑ toorimɔ.
bba	U nɛn sɑnu sɑnusu mɛɛrimɔ.
bba	nɑ rɑ nùn yɑ̃nu kɛ̃wɑ ni nɑ kuɑ kɑ nɛn yɑɑ
bba	sɑbenun sɑnsu u kɑ wooru yɑri.
bba	Mɑnɑ kon ɡoo wɑ u mɑn swɑɑ dɑki.
bba	Domi nɑ mɑɑri sere i kɑ bɛɛn ɡɑri kuɑ i kpɑ.
bba	Wee kon nɔɔ wukiɑ n ɡɑri ɡere.
bba	Gɑsɔ, u rɑ mɑɑ nùn sɛɛyɑsie kɑ wɑhɑlɑ,
bba	À kun mɑɑ ɡɛɛ mɔ ɑ ɡere, ɑ mɑn swɑɑ dɑkio.
bba	Gusunɔ ù n nɛɛ, u ǹ ɡoo ɡɑ̃ɑnu kuɑmmɛ, wɑrɑ koo

bba	Wɑrɑ u koo nɑ u bikiɑ ye n nun mɔ̀.
bba	wɑhɑlɑ kɑ nuku sɑnkirɑnun sɑɑ.
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u nɛɛ, wee, kon yibɛrɛbɑ seeyɑ bu Isirelibɑ
bba	mwɛɛri nɡe mɛ susure kowobu bɑ rɑ swɛ̃ɛ mwɛɛri.
bba	Yenibɑn biru, kon mɑɑ yibɛrɛ ɡɑbu seeyɑ bu bu wɔri bu
bba	ɡo ɡunɡunu wɔllɔ kɑ ɡuunɔ, kɑ sere mɑɑ kpee bɑɑbɑ
bba	sɔɔ nɡe mɛ tɑɑsobu bɑ rɑ yɛɛ wɔri bu ɡo.
bba	Kon bu ko ben yibɛrɛbɑn yobu,

bba	Yerusɑlɛmun ɡbɑ̃rɑ kɔnnɔsun di.
bba	Bɑ mɑn yinɑ bɛriɑ nɛn swɑɑ sɔɔ.
bba	Wunɛ Gusunɔ wɔllu kɑ tem Yinni,

bba	ɡe sɔɔ, tɔmbu kɑ yɑɑ sɑbenu.

bba	ɑ bu wisio ɑ nɛɛ, ɑmɛniwɑ nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔ nɑ ɡeruɑ.

bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u mɑɑ nɛɛ, u yɛ̃ himbɑ ye u yii bɛɛn
bba	sɔ̃. Himbɑ ɡeɑ, n ǹ mɔ himbɑ kɔ̃sɑ. U koo de ye i

bba	Isirelibɑn bweserɑ koo mɑɑ kpe,

bba	Yen sɔ̃, bɛsɛ kɑ bɛsɛn bibu sɑ Yonɑdɑbu, Rekɑbun biin

bba	Tem mɛ kpuro mu bɛrum duurɑ.

bba	mɑ yɑ kuɑ dɛkɑ yen nɛɛrɑ wunɔbu (500).
bba	Nɡe mɛyɑ sɔ̃ɔ nɔɔbɑ yiru yen bɑɑ sɔɔ bɑ koo kɑ
bba	yɑ̃ku yee te sɑ̃rɑsiɑ kpɑ tɑ n wɑ̃ɑ wi, Yinni
bba	Ye bɑ kɑ torɑrun yɑ̃kunu kɑ yɑ̃ku ni bɑ rɑ kɑ torɑnu
bba	sɔmɛ kuɑ kɑ kɛ̃ɛ ni bɑ kɑ nɑɑmɔ kɑ sere ye bɑ yi

bba	mɑɑ suru kpɑo bɑɑwure sɔɔ.

bba	koo nim wɔ̃kun nim dɛɛrɑsiɑ.
bba	Tem mɛ mu tie, mɛn yɑsum mu sɑ̃ɑwɑ ɡɔm soonu nɔrɔbun
bba	subɑ nɔɔbu (5.000). Mɑ mɛn dɛ̃ɛbu bu sɑ̃ɑ ɡɔm soonu
bba	nɔrɔbun subɑ yɛndɑ nɔɔbu (25.000). Ye kpuro yɑ ko n
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ wuuɡibuɡiɑ. Mɛ sɔɔrɑ bɑ koo ben diɑ bɑni

bba	U nɛɛ, nɑ nɛn yinni sinɑ bokon bɛrum mɔ. Domi wiyɑ u yi

bba	bɔɔru nɡe bɛɛɡii be bɑ tie, sɑɑ ye sɔɔ, kɑri
bba	sɔɔrɑ i mɑn doke mi. Domi bɑ koo kpĩ bu mɑn wiru burɑ.
bba	Yen biruwɑ Gusunɔ u Dɑniɛli dosu ɡe sɔ̃ɔwɑ wɔ̃kuru,

bba	ɑ sɑ̃ɑ nɡe wii wurɑɡii te. Wɔrukoowɑ u nun bɑndu kɑ

bba	mɛnnɔ yenɔ, kpɑ bu kɑ bɛɛ dɑ tem yɛ̃robu kɑ sinɑmbun
bba	wuswɑɑɔ nɛn sɔ̃ kpɑ i kɑ seedɑ di.
bba	domi bɑ ɡerumɔ bɑ mɔ̀, n ǹ weenɛ bu ko tɔ̃ɔ bɑkɑ
bba	te sɔɔ, kpɑ n ku rɑɑ ko ɡɑri bɑkɑ tɔmbun suunu sɔɔ.
bba	Adɑmɑ Piɛɛ u nɔɔ ɡɛ̃ɛ dim dim u mɔ̀, nɑ ǹ nun
bba	sikimɔ pɑi. Bɑɑ ǹ n ɡɔɔn nɑ, sɑnnɑ sɑ ko ɡbi.
bba	Kɑ mɛ, bɑɑ ɡɑri yinin tii sɔɔ bɑ ǹ nɔɔ tiɑ kue.
bba	Yerɑ bɑ kpɑm ɡbɑ̃sukum wɔri bɑ nɛɛ, ɑ nùn kpɑreo
bba	N deemɑ beyɑ bɑ rɑɑ Yesu swĩi bɑ nùn nɔɔrimɔ sɑnɑm
bba	mɛ u wɑ̃ɑ Gɑlileɔ. Kurɔbu dɑbiru ɡɑrɑ mɑɑ wɑ̃ɑ
bba	mi, be bɑ kɑ nùn nɑ Yerusɑlɛmuɔ sɑnnu.
bba	N wee sɑnɑm mɛ n ben wuuru ɡirɑri, Sɑkɑri win yɑ̃ku
bba	kobun sɔmburu mɔ̀ Gusunɔn wuswɑɑɔ.
bba	Sɔ̃ɔ mɛɛ te sɔɔ, Mɑɑri u seewɑ kpɑɑkɑ u dɑ Yudeɑn
bba	wuu ɡɑɡu sɔɔ ɡe ɡɑ wɑ̃ɑ ɡuunun berɑ ɡiɑ.
bba	Mɑ bɑ nɛɛ, wunɛn bweseru sɔɔ, ɡoo sɑri wi u yĩsi te
bba	wɑ bɑ̀ n bu ben torɑnu suuru kuɑ
bba	Mɑ yɑ̃ɑ kpɑro be, bɑ ɡɔsirɑ bɑ Gusunɔ bɛɛrɛ
bba	wɛ̃ɛmɔ, bɑ nùn siɑrɑmɔ yɑbu ye kpuron sɔ̃ ye bɑ
bba	nuɑ kɑ ye bɑ wɑ, nɡe mɛ ɡɔrɑdo wi, u rɑɑ bu
bba	Mɑ u bu bikiɑ u nɛɛ, mbɑ n kuɑ i kɑ mɑn kɑsu. I ǹ
bba	yɛ̃ mɑ nɑ ǹ kon ko nɑ kun nɛn bɑɑbɑn wunɑnɔsu kue?
bba	Mɑ Herodu u kpɑm dɑɑ kɔ̃sɑ ye sɔɔ dɑɑ kɔ̃sɑ sosi,
bba	u derɑ bɑ Yohɑnu pirisɔm doke.
bba	Yesu u nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, Gusunɔn ɡɑri mɑɑ nɛɛ,
bba	“A ku rɑ Gusunɔ wunɛn Yinnin dɑm mɛɛri ɑ kɑ wɑ mɛ mu
bba	Mɑ win lɑbɑɑri yɑ nɔɔrɑ n kɑ sikerenɑ berɑ ye sɔɔ
bba	Adɑmɑ Yesu u ben bwisikunu ɡiɑ mɑ u bu bikiɑ u nɛɛ,
bba	mbɑn sɔ̃nɑ i bwisikumɔ mɛ bɛɛn ɡɔ̃ruɔ.
bba	Ye u ɡu dɛmiɑ, mɑ ɡɑ bɛkurɑ.
bba	I kun dɑ n tɔmbu sirimɔ, Gusunɔ u ǹ mɑɑ kɑ bɛɛ
bba	sirimɔ. I kun dɑ n tɔmbu tɑɑrɛ wɛ̃ɛmɔ, Gusunɔ u ǹ
bba	mɑɑ bɛɛ tɑɑrɛ wɛ̃ɛmɔ. I suuru koowo, Gusunɔ koo
bba	Yohɑnun bwɑ̃ɑbɑ nùn ye kpuron lɑbɑɑri sɔ̃ɔwɑ. Mɑ u
bba	A ǹ mɑn tɔburɑ kɑ sɔ̃subu, ɑdɑmɑ kurɔ wini, mìn di
bba	nɑ duɑ, u ǹ nɛn nɑɑsu sɔ̃sum deri.
bba	Bɑ nùn susi mɑ bɑ nùn yɑmiɑ bɑ nɛɛ, Yinni, Yinni, sɑ
bba	Yesu u ye nuɑ, mɑ u nùn sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɑ ku bɛrum ko,

bba	kun kɑ bɛɛ yibɛrɛ tɛɛru nɛni, bɛɛɡiiwɑ.

bba	N wee durɔ ɡoo wìn wɑsi yi mɔsɑ u yɔ̃ Yesun wuswɑɑɔ.

bba	U yobun turo sokɑ u bikiɑ mbɑ n kuɑ.

bba	Be kpuro bɑ nɛɛ, ǹ n mɑn nɑ wunɛ Gusunɔn Biiwɑ?
bba	Tɔn wɔru ɡunɑ yɑ nùn swĩi. Ye sɔɔ, tɔn kurɔbu ɡɑbɑ
bba	wɑ̃ɑ be bɑ sumɔ bɑ kpɑsɑ wɔri mɔ̀ win sɔ̃.

bba	rɑɑ mɔ. Nɑ yɛ̃ kɑm kɑm mɑ ɑ mɑɑ bu mɔ.
bba	Yeni kpurowɑ kɑɑ wunɛn tɔmbu yɑɑyɑsiɑ kpɑ ɑ mɑɑ bu
bba	kirɔ ko Gusunɔn wuswɑɑɔ bu ku sikirinɑ ɡɑri wɛ̃ɛrinun
bba	sɔ̃. Domi yenin bweserɑ kun ɑrufɑɑni ɡɑɑ mɔ mɑ n kun
bba	mɔ yu tɔmbu kɑm koosiɑ be bɑ swɑɑ dɑki.
bba	Nɑ nun yiiremɔ kɑ ɡem Gusunɔn wuswɑɑɔ kɑ Kirisi Yesun
bba	wuswɑɑɔ wi u koo wɑsobu kɑ ɡɔribu siri, nɑ mɑɑ nun
bba	yiiremɔ win wurɑmɑru kɑ win bɑndun sɔ̃,
bba	Domi tɔn bɛrɛtɛkɛ dɑbinu wɑ̃ɑ kɑ wiirɑ ɡɑri ɡerobu
bba	kɑ be bɑ tɔmbu nɔni wɔ̃kumɔ, n kun mɑm ko Yuubɑ.
bba	Nɑ kĩ ɑ yi ɡere ɑ sire kpɑ be bɑ Gusunɔ nɑɑnɛ doke bu
bba	ben sɑɑ di sɔm ɡeenun kobu sɔɔ. Gɑri yi, yi wɑ̃ yi
bba	mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ tɔmbun ɑrufɑɑni.
bba	Mɛyɑ mɑɑ nɛn sɔm kowosibu Mɑɑku kɑ Aritɑɑki kɑ
bba	Demɑsi kɑ sere Luku, bɑ nun tɔburɑ.
bba	Kpɑ u mɑɑ kɑ bu yɑkiɑ be bɑ sɑ̃ɑ nɡe yobu ben
bba	wɑ̃ɑru kpuro sɔɔ ɡɔɔn bɛrum sɔ̃.
bba	Nɡe mɛyɑ Kirisi kun tii yɑ̃ku kowo tɔnwerorun yiiko wɛ̃.
bba	Gusunɔwɑ u nùn ye wɛ̃ wi u nɛɛ,
bba	Nɡe mɛyɑ Gusunɔ u kĩɑ u be bɑ koo kɛ̃ru mwɑ te u bu
bba	nɔɔ mwɛɛru kuɑ sɔ̃ɔsi kpɑsɑsɑ mɑ win ɡɑri kun
bba	kɔbiɑrɔ. Yen sɔ̃nɑ u nɔɔ mwɛɛru kuɑ u sire kɑ
bba	Yen sɔ̃nɑ Yesu kɑ sun nɔɔ mwɛɛru nɑɑwɑ te tɑ burɑm
bba	sɑɑ bii piimunun di sere kɑ bukurobɔ.
bba	Nɡe mɛ Gusunɔ u bɑɑwure bure u ɡbi nɔn teeru u sere nùn
bba	U sun swɑɑ kpɑɑ yɑbɑ ye yɑ wɑsi sɑɑ kɑrerun min di te
bba	N deemɑ ɡoo sɑri wìn kookoosu koo Gusunɔ wɛ̃re n kun kɑ
bba	nɑɑnɛ dokebu. Geemɑ, wi u Gusunɔ susimɔ u nɑɑnɛ sɑ̃ɑ
bba	mɑ Gusunɔ u wɑ̃ɑ mɑ u rɑ be bɑ nùn kɑsu durom kue.
bba	Bɑ ɡɑbu tɔ̃yɑ kuɑ bɑ kɑ ɡo. Bɑ yinɑ bu bu fɑɑbɑ
bba	ko bu kɑ wɑ bu se bu du wɑ̃ɑru sɔɔ te tɑ burɑm bo.
bba	Adɑmɑ bɛɛ, Siɔnin ɡuurɑ i susi kɑ Gusunɔ Yinni wɑson
bba	wuu ɡe ɡɑ sɑ̃ɑ Yerusɑlɛmu wɔrukɑɑ, kɑ ɡen ɡɔrɑdo
bba	dɑbi dɑbiru te tɑ ǹ ɡɑrirɔ te tɑ mɛnnɛ kɑ nuku dobu.
bba	Gusunɔ wi u ɑlɑfiɑ wɛ̃ɛmɔ u bɛsɛn Yinni Yesu seeyɑ
bba	ɡɔrin di, mɑ Yesu wi, u kuɑ bɛsɛn yɑ̃ɑ kpɑro boko win
bba	yɛm sɔ̃ mɛ mu nɔɔ mwɛɛ te tɑ ku rɑ kpen ɡɑri sire.
bba	Goo ù n tɑmɑɑ u Gusunɔ sɑ̃ɑmɔ mɑ u ǹ win yɑrɑ
bba	kpĩɑ, u tii weesu kuɑmmɛwɑ, win sɑ̃ɑru kɑmɑ.
bba	Sɑ rɑ dumi yɑruki dokeye yi kɑ sun mɛm nɔɔwɑ. Nɡe
bba	mɛyɑ sɑ ko kpĩ su yin wɑsi kpuro ɡɔsikiɑ.
bba	Domi i ǹ yɛ̃ ye bɛɛn wɑ̃ɑrɑ ko n sɑ̃ɑ siɑ. I
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ nɡe bukɔ ɡe ɡɑ rɑ wɔrumɛ sɑɑ fiiko sɔɔ,
bba	Lɑɑkɑri mɛɛri bi, bu bɛɛn nɑɑnɛ dokebu wɛ̃ɛrimɔ.
bba	Nɡe mɛ bɑ rɑ wurɑ mɛɛri kɑ dɔ̃ɔ, bɑɑ mɛ yɑ koo
bba	kɑm ko, nɡe mɛyɑ bɑ bɛɛn nɑɑnɛ dokebu mɛɛrimɔ, bi
bba	bu wurɑ bɛɛrɛ kere ɡem ɡem, bu kɑ bin dɑm ɡiɑ. Kpɑ i
bba	siɑrɑbu kɑ yiiko kɑ bɛɛrɛ wɑ sɑnɑm mɛ Kirisi koo
bba	nɑ tu kuɑ ɡɑni ɡɔmburun dɑm Siɔniɔ.
bba	Nɡe mɛyɑ yellun tɔn kurɔ be bɑ Gusunɔ sɑ̃ɑmɔ mɑ bɑ
bba	nùn yĩiyɔ, bɑ rɑ rɑɑ tii sɔmɛ, mɑ bɑ ben durɔbu wiru
bba	Bɑɑyere kpuron kpeeru tɑ turuku kuɑ. Ǹ n mɛn nɑ, i tii
bba	nɛnuɔ kɑ lɑɑkɑri, kpɑ i se i yɔ̃rɑ i kɑ kpĩ i
bba	Bɛɛ be Yesu Kirisi bɛsɛn Yinni kɑ bɛsɛn Fɑɑbɑ kowo
bba	ɡeeɡii u nɑɑnɛ dokebu wɛ̃ nɡe bɛsɛ, nɛ Simɔɔ
bba	Piɛɛ, win yoo kɑ win ɡɔro, nɛnɑ nɑ bɛɛ tire te
bba	n mɑm nɛɛre be bɑ ben wɑsin kĩru kɑnkɑm mɔ̀ mɑ bɑ
bba	Adɑmɑ bɛɛ nɛn kĩnɑsibu i ɡɑ̃ɑ ni yɛ̃ kɔ. Ǹ n
bba	mɛn nɑ, i n tii sɛ kpɑ i ku de i kɔ̃ɔrɑ i wɔrumɑ be
bba	bɑ ǹ Gusunɔn bɛɛrɛ yɛ̃n torɑrun sɔ̃.
bba	Adɑmɑ bɛɛ i Hunde Dɛɛro mwɑ Kirisin min di mɑ bɛɛ
bba	Yen sɔ̃, nɛn kĩnɑsibu, bɛsɛn ɡɔ̃ru ɡɑ̀ kun sun
bba	tɑɑrɛ wɛ̃ɛmɔ, sɑ ko n toro sindu mɔ Gusunɔn wuswɑɑɔ.
bba	Wi u hɑnduniɑ kɑmiɑmɔ, wiyɑ wi u nɑɑnɛ doke mɑ Yesu
bba	Gɑyusi, wunɛ wi nɑ kĩ kɑ ɡem, nɛ wi nɑ sɑ̃ɑ Yesun
bba	yiɡbɛ ɡuro ɡuro, nɛnɑ nɑ nun tɔburɑ.
bba	Asoru u Sɑdɔku mɑrɑ. Sɑdɔku u Asimu mɑrɑ. Asimu u Eliudu
bba	Ye kperin sɑriɑ yɛ̃ro be, bɑ biru kisi bɑ doonɑ, mɑ
bba	Yinnin ɡɔrɑdo u Yosɛfu kure dosu sɔɔ u nɛɛ, ɑ seewo ɑ
bba	bii wi kɑ win mɛro suɑ kpɑ ɑ kɑ bu kpikiru su Eɡibiti
bba	ɡiɑ, ɑ sinɑ mi sere dɔmɑ te kon mɑɑ nun sɔ̃ ɑ
bba	sĩimɑ, domi Herodu u koo bii wi kɑsu u ɡo.
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛyɑ Yesu u nɑ sɑɑ Gɑlilen di u dɑ dɑɑ te bɑ
bba	mɔ̀ Yuudɛniɔ, Yohɑnu u kɑ nùn bɑtɛmu ko.
bba	Mii mii bɑ ben yɑ̃ɑkoronu deri, mɑ bɑ nùn swĩi.
bba	Nɡe mɛyɑ i de bɛɛn yɑm bururɑm mu bururɑ tɔmbun
bba	wuswɑɑɔ kpɑ bɑ n kɑ bɛɛn sɔm ɡeenu wɑɑmɔ, kpɑ bu
bba	wɑ bu bɛɛn Bɑɑbɑ wɔrukoo bɛɛrɛ wɛ̃.
bba	Ì n mɑɑ bɛɛɡibu tɔnɑ tɔburɑ, sɑnɔ yerɑ̀ i ɡɑbu
bba	kere. Tɔn tukobun tii mɑm, bɑ rɑ ko mɛ.
bba	Yesu mɑɑ nɛɛ, yen sɔ̃, i ku wururɑ kɑ dĩɑnun ɡɑri,
bba	ǹ kun mɛ ye i ko nɔ i n kɑ wɑ̃ɑ, ǹ kun mɛ ye i ko
bba	bɛɛn wɑsi wukiri. Wɑ̃ɑru tɑ dĩɑnu kere, wɑsi mɑɑ yi
bba	Yesu mɑɑ nɛɛ, n ǹ mɔ bɑɑwure wi u mɑn sokumɔ Yinni,
bba	Yinni, wiyɑ u koo du mi Gusunɔ u bɑndu swĩi, mɑ n kun mɔ
bba	wi u nɛn Bɑɑbɑ wi u wɑ̃ɑ wɔllɔn kĩru mɔ̀.
bba	Yesu u nùn wisɑ u nɛɛ, sɛmusu bweusu mɔ, ɡunɔsu su mɑɑ
bba	sokunu mɔ. Adɑmɑ nɛ Tɔnun Bii nɑ ǹ nɛn tii ɑyeru
bba	Yesu u ben ɡɑri yi nuɑ mɑ u nɛɛ, be bɑ bwɑ̃ɑ do bɑ
bba	ǹ timɡiin bukɑtɑ mɔ mɑ n kun mɔ be bɑ bɑrɔ.
bba	Yesu u win bwɑ̃ɑbu wɔkurɑ yiru mɛnnɑ mɑ u bu yiiko wɛ̃
bba	bu kɑ wɛrɛkunu ɡirɑ, kpɑ bu bɑrɑru kɑ wɑsin dɑm
bba	Ǹ n mɛn nɑ, i ku bɛrum ko, i ɡunɔminu bɛɛrɛ kere sere
bba	Tɔnun Bii mɑɑ nɑ u dimɔ u nɔrumɔ, mɑ bɑ ɡerumɔ bɑ
bba	mɔ̀ u sɑ̃ɑ dim kĩro kɑ tɑm nɔro, kɑ mɑɑ ɡbere
bba	mwɑɔbu kɑ kɔ̃sɑn kowobun bɔrɔ. Kɑ mɛ, Gusunɔn bwisi
bba	yi rɑ sɔ̃ɔsi mɑ yi sɑ̃ɑ ɡem yin kookoosun di.
bba	Gɑri yi sɔɔ, Gusunɔ u nɛɛ,
bba	Siribun sɑnɑm sɔɔ Ninifuɡibu bɑ koo tɛ̃n tɔmbu seesi bu
bba	bu tɑɑrɛ wɛ̃ domi bɑ ben wɑ̃ɑru ɡɔsiɑ Yonɑsin
bba	wɑɑsun sɔ̃. Wee tɛ̃ ɡɑ̃ɑnu wɑ̃ɑ mini ni nu Yonɑsi
bba	Kpɑ bu ku ɡiɑ kɑ ben bwisi.
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ sɔɔrɑ be bɑ kuɑ ye Gusunɔ u bikiɑ bɑ ko n
bba	bɑllimɔ nɡe sɔ̃ɔ mi ben Bɑɑbɑ u bɑndu swĩi. Wi u
bba	swɑɑ mɔ u kɑ nɔ, u nɔɔwɔ.
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ sɔ̃ɔ duɔ win bwɑ̃ɑbɑ nɑ win mi bɑ nɛɛ,
bba	wee, ɡbɑburu sɔɔrɑ sɑ wɑ̃ɑ mini, sɔ̃ɔ mɑɑ kpɑ. A
bba	tɔn be kɑro bu dɑ bɑru kpɑɑnɔ bu ben tii dĩɑnu dwiɑ.
bba	Murɑfiti bɛɛ, kɑ ɡeemɑ bɛɛn sɔ̃nɑ Gusunɔ u ɡeruɑ
bba	Yesu bu bikiɑ u nɛɛ, pɛ̃ɛ nyewɑ i sere mɔ.
bba	Adɑmɑ Yesu sĩirɑ u Piɛɛ sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɑ ɡɛɛro
bba	nɛn birun di Setɑm. A kɑsu ɑ mɑn torɑsiɑwɑ, domi ɑ ǹ
bba	bwisikumɔ nɡe Gusunɔ, mɑ n kun mɔ nɡe tɔnu.
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ Yesu kɑ win bwɑ̃ɑbu bɑ turɑ Kɑpenɑmuɔ,
bba	yerɑ sɑ̃ɑ yerun wɔ̃ɔ ɡobiɡibɑ nɑ Piɛɛn mi bɑ
bba	nɛɛ, bɛɛn yinni u ku rɑ sɑ̃ɑ yerun wɔ̃ɔ ɡobi kɔsie?
bba	Wee, durɔ wi kun ɡɑ̃ɑnu mɔ u kɑ dii bi kɔsiɑ. Mɑ win
bba	yinni nɛɛ bu nùn dɔro kɑ win kurɔ kɑ win bibu kɑ ye u
bba	mɔ kpuro bu kɑ dii bi kɔsiɑ.
bba	ɑ wunɛn tundo kɑ wunɛn mɛro bɛɛrɛ wɛ̃ɛyɔ, kpɑ ɑ
bba	wunɛn tɔnusi kĩɑ nɡe wunɛn tii tii.
bba	kpɑ bu nùn tɔn tukobu nɔmu sɔndiɑ be bɑ koo nùn
bba	yɑɑkoru ko, bu nùn sɛni so, yen biru bu nùn kpɑre dɑ̃ɑ
bba	bunɑnɑrɔ. Sɔ̃ɔ itɑse u koo mɑɑ se ɡɔrin di.
bba	Yesu u duɑ sɑ̃ɑ yerɔ mɑ u be bɑ kiɑru dɔrɑmɔ kɑ be
bba	bɑ dwemɔ ɡirɑ min di. U be bɑ ɡobi kɔsimɔn tɑbulubɑ
bba	fukurɑ, kɑ totobɛrɛ dɔrobun kitɑnu.
bba	Yɛnu yɛ̃ro wi, u kpɑm bu ɡɑbu ɡɔriɑ be bɑ ɡbiikobu
bba	dɑbiru kere. Dɑɑ tiɑ yerɑ bɑ ben tii kuɑ.
bba	Adɑmɑ Yesu u ben bwisi kɔ̃si yi yɛ̃ mɑ u bu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u
bba	nɛɛ, murɑfiti bɛɛ! Mbɑn sɔ̃nɑ i kĩ i nɛn lɑɑkɑri
bba	Bɛɛ woodɑ yɛ̃robu kɑ Fɑlisibɑ murɑfiti bɛɛ, i ko
bba	nɔni swɑ̃ɑru wɑ! Domi i kɑ sikinu weenɛ ni bɑ soo
bba	tɛɛni. Nin wɔllɑ wɑ̃ ɑdɑmɑ sɔɔwɔ ɡonun kukunɑ nu
bba	yibɑ kɑ yɑbu bɑɑyere ye yɑ kɔ̃sɑ.
bba	Wi u mɑɑ woo ɡberɔ u ku ɡɔsirɑ yɛnuɔ u kɑ win kumbooro
bba	Adɑmɑ ù n sɑ̃ɑ sɔm kowo kɑm, mɑ u bwisikumɔ u mɔ̀,
bba	Ǹ n mɛn nɑ, n dɑɑ weenɛwɑ ɑ nɛn ɡobi ɡoo wɛ̃ kɑ
bba	nim kɛ̃ru, sɑnɑm mɛ nɑ wumɑ kpɑ n nɛnyɑm wɑ kɑ ɑre.
bba	Domi bɑɑdommɑwɑ sɑ̃ɑrobɑ wɑ̃ɑ kɑ bɛɛ, ɑdɑmɑ
bba	nɛnɑ, nɑ ǹ ko nɑ n wɑ̃ɑ kɑ bɛɛ bɑɑdommɑ.
bba	Yerɑ u bu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, nɛn nukurɑ sɑnkirɑ sere n
bba	ɡɔɔ ɡum ɡirɑri. I yɔ̃ro mini i kɑ mɑn dom se.
bba	Yerɑ yɑ̃ku kowo tɔnwero u win tiin yɑberu nɛnuɑ u
bba	kɑrɑnɑ mɔrun sɔ̃ mɑ u nɛɛ, u Gusunɔ ɡɑri kɑm
bba	ɡerusi, seedɑɡii berɑ̀ sɑ kpɑm mɑrɑ. I nuɑ tɛ̃
bba	N deemɑ sɑɑ ye sɔɔ, pirisɔm yĩsiruɡii ɡoo wɑ̃ɑ mi,
bba	U Gusunɔ nɑɑnɛ sɑ̃ɑ mɑ u nɛɛ, wiyɑ Gusunɔn Bii. Ǹ
bba	n mɛn nɑ, Gusunɔ u nùn fɑɑbɑ koowo ù n nùn kĩ.
bba	kpɑ i dɑ fuuku fuuku i win bwɑ̃ɑbu sɔ̃ mɑ u seewɑ
bba	ɡɔrin di. Wee, u bɛɛ ɡbiiyɔ u dɔɔ Gɑlileɔ. Miyɑ i ko
bba	nùn wɑ. Yerɑ nɑ bɛɛ sɔ̃ɔbu nɑ.
bba	Tɔn be, bɑ rɑ n wure, ɡɑ̃ɑnu sɑri ni nu rɑ bu wɛ̃re,
bba	ben binɛ bu kpɑre. Bɑ rɑ woo kɑnɑ ɡɑri ɡere, bɑ mɑɑ
bba	tɔmbu ɡɑri dori sɔ̃ɔmɔ bu kɑ yɛ̃robun ɡɑ̃ɑnu wɑ.
bba	Kirisi u Yohɑnu sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɑ Efesun Yesun yiɡbɛrun
bba	ɡɔrɑdo yoruo ɑ nɛɛ, nɛ wi nɑ kperi nɔɔbɑ yiru ye
bba	nɛni nɛn nɔm ɡeuɔ, mɑ nɑ sĩimɔ dɑbu wurɑɡinu
bba	nɔɔbɑ yiru yen suunu sɔɔ nɑ nɛɛ,
bba	Bɑɑwure wi u swɑɑ mɔ u nɔɔwɔ ye Hunde Dɛɛro u Yesun
bba	Sinɑ kitɑ ten suunu sɔɔ kɑ ten ɡɔn ɡɔnkɑ, hunde
bba	konibɑ nnɛ bɑ wɑ̃ɑ mi, bɑ nɔni dɑbinu mɔ biru kɑ
bba	Bɑ koo bɑndu di hɑnduniɑ kpuro sɔɔ.
bba	Nɑ mɑɑ wɔllun ɡɔrɑdo ɡoo wɑ u wee sɑɑ sɔ̃ɔ yɑri
bba	yerun di, u Gusunɔ Yinni wɑson yĩreru nɛni. U ɡɔrɑdobɑ
bba	nnɛ ye nɔɔɡiru kuɑ be Gusunɔ u dɑm kɑ̃ bu kɑ tem kɑ
bba	Yen biru ɡɔrɑdo nɔɔbuse u win kɔbɑ so. Mɑ nɑ kperɑ wɑ
bba	ye yɑ rɑɑ wɔrumɑ temɔ sɑɑ wɔllun di, bɑ ye wɔru
bba	bɔkɔ nɔru sɑriruɡuun kɔkɔrɔ wɛ̃.
bba	Nɑ tire kure piibu ɡe mwɑ win nɔmun di, mɑ nɑ ɡu temɑ.
bba	Geemɑ, nɛn nɔɔwɔ ɡɑ dorɑwɑ nɡe tim, ɑdɑmɑ ye nɑ
bba	ɡu mwɛ nɑ kpɑ, ɡɑ sosiɑwɑ dɑkɑ dɑkɑ nɛn nukurɔ.
bba	kɑ be bɑ wunɛn yĩsiru nɑsie, bɑkɑ kɑ buu.
bba	Ǹ n mɛn nɑ, bɑɑwure wi u swɑɑ mɔ, u nɔɔwɔ.
bba	Yen biru, nɑ kpɑm yĩreru ɡɑru wɑ Gusunɔ wɔllɔ, tɑ
bba	kpɑ̃ mɑ tɑ bɛrum mɔ. Ye nɑ wɑ wee. Wɔllun ɡɔrɑdobɑ
bba	nɔɔbɑ yiru bɑ ɡbee swɑ̃ɑnu nɔɔbɑ yiru nɛni. Niyɑ nu
bba	sɑ̃ɑ ɡbee swɑ̃ɑ dɑ̃ɑkinu, domi ni sɔɔrɑ Gusunɔn
bba	Mɑ Yesun nɔɔ ɡɑ nɔɔrɑ u nɛɛ, wee, nɑ sisi nɡe
bba	ɡbɛnɔ. Doo nɔɔruɡiiwɑ wi u swɑɑ mɛɛrɑ mɑ u win
bba	yɑ̃nu kpɑrenu sɑ̃ɑ u ku kɑ swɑɑ wɔri tereru kpɑ u
bba	Domi yen durum yɑ wɔllu ɡirɑri, mɑ Gusunɔ u yen kom
bba	U mɑɑ mɑn sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɡɑri yi, Gusunɔn ɡɑri
bba	Mɑ nɑ wuu dɛɛrɔ wɑ, ɡe ɡɑ sɑ̃ɑ Yerusɑlɛmu kpɑɑ,
bba	ɡɑ sɑrɑm wee Gusunɔ wɔllun di, ɡɑ sɔɔru sɑ̃ɑ nɡe
bba	kurɔ kpɑo wi u burɑru sɑ̃ɑ u win durɔ mɑrɑ.
bba	Gusunɔ kɑ Yɑ̃ɑ kinɛ kpɛm ten sinɑ turɑrɑ tɑ ko n
bba	wɑ̃ɑ mi, kpɑ win sɔm kowobu bu nùn sɑ̃.
